Spanish Rebels Resist Stubbornly Government Faces Life-and-Death Crisis Builds Fortifications in Guadarrama Mountains Scattered Bandits Rise Up in the West and Loot Rampantly 63

Madrid Army Minister General Miajas recently went to the Guadarrama Mountain front north of the capital to decorate military affairs. Once preparations are complete, he will order an attack on the northern rebels who are stubbornly resisting. It is reported that only eight hundred troops remain of rebels near the Leon Pass in the Guadarrama Mountains. After occupying the mountain pass, the government army moved artillery to the summit and fired down from a high position, inflicting heavy losses on the rebel artillery. As for the air force, the rebels only have three old-fashioned planes stationed in Burgos, which is far inferior to the government army. Government aircraft flew to the rebel positions last night to bomb them, and machine gun teams arrived shortly after, further strengthening the government army's momentum. (27th Havas Dispatch)

Lisbon According to radio reports from various sources, the rebels now control thirty provinces and parts of three other provinces, while the government controls sixteen provinces and parts of one other province. (26th National Electricity)

Madrid Government forces are fighting fierce battles with the Fascist Party, Royalist Party, and other right-wing rebels in more than four major battles and twenty minor battles across the country today. Major battles occurred in Oviedo, Seville, and the mountain passes of Zaragoza. The number of deaths is uncertain. Communist riots occurred in Hellera, Malaga, Pogeseda, and Albacin, engaging in murder and arson. Thousands of farmers, led by worker leader Founante, besieged the rebels in Oviedo today. Founte said he would spare no sacrifice to eradicate the rebels. The government considers the northern battles to be decisive and has sent General Gasde to command military affairs in the Sierra Pass. The government announced a great victory in Somashira, but in reality, government forces and rebels have had victories and defeats. According to unofficial news, the government army has now occupied the Ardul Turon mountainous area and is building fortifications. A company of female soldiers is rushing to support them, preventing the advance of General Mura's troops. (26th National Electricity)

(London) As the struggle between the Spanish government and the rebels is at a critical juncture, scattered bandits have risen up in various parts of the western border, causing the usual state of terror during local chaos. It is said that the behavior of these scattered bandits is extremely brutal and terrifying. According to refugees who fled from Badajoz in western Spain into Portugal, yesterday, groups of communists broke into the homes of more than a hundred landowners, first insulting their wives and daughters, then cutting off one ear of each homeowner before leaving. Extreme panic has occurred in Vigo, a famous seaport on the west coast of Spain, and all wealthy homes have been looted. (27th Reuters Dispatch)

Madrid General Faras, commander of the Spanish government army, told General Gabanilas, commander of the rebels resisting in Zaragoza, "I order you to surrender the city." Mr. Jia replied, "I will never surrender." The two sides are currently engaged in fierce fighting to争该城, the government army has established an air base in Lireda, eighty miles from the city, from which they have repeatedly sent aircraft to bomb the beautiful ancient city, causing heavy damage. There are currently three other dangerous areas outside Madrid: one is Seville, and a column of government troops is advancing towards the city; one is Albayete, 138 miles southeast of the capital. If the government army can occupy the city, the capital's food supply can be guaranteed; one is San Sebastian, a resort in northern Spain, where government forces are gradually gaining ground around it. (26th Reuters Dispatch)

Government Forces Occupy Victory in the Vicinity of Kin畿 Rebels Retreat to Segovia Food Shortage Panic in the Capital Slightly Reduced 64

Madrid Although the Spanish government troops have repelled the rebels threatening Madrid, causing them to retreat to Segovia, forty miles from the western capital, General Franco, the leader of the rebels, told a Reuters reporter in Tangier, Spanish Morocco, that the turmoil is progressing well. He said that the Foreign Legion and indigenous troops have all joined us and are willing to fight to the last man. My headquarters will soon move to Seville. The supply of food and water to Madrid is now in our hands, but we have not yet cut it off. The panic of food shortage in Madrid has decreased due to the government's victory, especially the recovery of Albayete, because communication with Valencia has been restored. The western capital is now more stable than before, and all troops have set out to fight. Women loyal to the government are doing their best to organize a "company of female soldiers" to help men engage in war. In addition to defeating the rebels and causing them to retreat to Segovia, government troops have also gained control of the key points in the Guadarrama Mountains. (27th Reuters Dispatch)

Northern War Situation: People's Militia of 8,000 Formed into Three Columns, Attacking Saragossa City from Different Routes 65

Barcelona: Saragossa City, the capital of Aragon province in the north, is still in the hands of the rebels. A people's militia of 8,500 men has been formed into three columns and are advancing on the city from different routes. The first column, with 3,000 men, is led by the anti-rebel leader and commander-in-chief of the workers' militia, Falla. After occupying Lerida City, they are moving up the Ebro River and have now reached the town of Mina, 35 kilometers from Saragossa City (along the Ebro River), forming the central route. The second column, totaling 2,000 men, set out from Tarragona City, first occupied Salinena City, and have now reached Tiedienta, 60 kilometers from Saragossa City, forming the northern route. The third column, totaling 3,500 men, is a mixed force composed of the 16th Infantry Regiment and artillery militia. After occupying Gasper City, they have now reached Alganis City, 50 kilometers from Saragossa City, forming the southern route. In addition, air force personnel are flying multiple aircraft to assist in the suppression, conducting bombing raids. It is reported that the rebel commander of Aragon province has telegraphed Yega and Huesca (both north of Saragossa City and in the hands of the rebels) for assistance. A fortress in Yega City has suffered significant damage after being bombed by aircraft. Huesca City is also surrounded by government troops, with white flags hoisted, but the rebels in both locations have not surrendered and are still resisting. Today is a holiday, and although the city is in the midst of war, members of the People's Front militia, either on foot or in cars, are parading through the streets, holding high the flags of their respective party groups and trade unions. However, everything appears as usual. The playgrounds are closed, and many citizens are visiting the site of the fierce battle that took place last Sunday to commemorate the ruins. (Havas dispatch, 26th)

Summary of War News from Various Sources: Government Air Force Carries Out Extensive Bombardments 66

Madrid: Regarding the current situation in Spain, the positions held by the government forces show slight progress, but the final outcome is still uncertain. According to government reports, the air force of the Autonomous Region of Catalonia flew to Palma, Majorca Island (in the Balearic Islands in the Mediterranean), and bombed the rebel forces there. Rebel leaders fled in small boats and were captured by submarine crew members loyal to the government. It is also rumored that General Gabanas, the rebel commander of Navarre province (near the French border), is in a dire situation. He has shaved his beard and changed his clothes to easily hide if necessary. Many of his rebel troops have fled into France. General Mola's rebel troops, the Northern Front commander, suffered 2,000 casualties in the Battle of the Guadarrama Pass, north of the capital. In Badajoz City in the west (near the Portuguese border), many right-wing leaders have fled into Portugal. Small groups of rebels, along with their wives and children, are entrenched in the nearby cities of Argalazai (southeast of the capital) and Toledo (south of the capital) and have not retreated. The People's Front party troops have urged them to surrender to avoid attack by government forces and to preserve the lives of their families. However, if the rebels refuse, they would rather die with their wives and children than surrender to government troops. As for Morocco in Africa, the government air force was ordered this afternoon to fly over Melilla and Ceuta and carry out bombings, inflicting heavy losses on the rebels. It is reported that they intend to abandon their original plan and no longer cross the Strait of Gibraltar. The Ministry of the Interior has also issued a statement saying that the government forces have defeated the rebels in various locations, and the situation has greatly improved today. It also stated that wherever the government forces go, the local people and the government air force can cooperate sincerely, so the results are very significant. In addition, the government bulletin has issued an order that retired military officers who have served the republican system effectively and have outstanding achievements can be reinstated to their original positions. The method of regulating food supplies in the capital has been designated and implemented by the governor of Madrid Province. All food and chemicals are prohibited from being exported, and export licenses that expire on July 31st are specially extended to remain valid. (Havas dispatch, 26th)

Madrid: The government announced in a broadcast last night that the government forces had won a victory in the Sumosan area (70 kilometers north of the capital), immediately occupied important positions, and sent multiple aircraft to pursue the rebels in the air with bombs. The rebel forces in Saragossa City in the north have been driven into a dead end and will soon be captured in one fell swoop. After the port of Palma on Majorca Island in the Mediterranean fell into the hands of the rebels, the government sent aircraft to bomb it, and the rebels there will soon surrender. Traffic between the capital and the southeastern provinces has been restored. A train of freight cars that left Valencia port arrived in the capital today. Passenger trains between the capital and Cartagena port, the capital and Cuenca City, the capital and Puertollano City, and between Barcelona City and Valencia port have also resumed normal service. Daily life in the capital has returned to normal since yesterday. A column of the People's Militia that was sent to Avila City (northwest of the capital) to suppress the Northern Front rebels returned yesterday, and the citizens welcomed them warmly. The Naval Department received a telegram from the captain of the warship "General Ferrándiz" regarding news from the rebel forces in Tetuan, Morocco, and emphatically denied the rumor that the ship had sunk. In addition, Minister of the Army General Miaja is scheduled to inspect the positions on the Guadarrama front in the north today. Other miscellaneous news is summarized as follows: (1) The security team of Castuera Village in Badajoz Province in the west, which had previously defected, has now returned to the government side. (2) Cartagena Port in the southeast, which was previously occupied by the rebels, has been captured by government troops after a fierce battle. (3) Colonel Villanueva, the commander of the first column under General Mola, the commander of the Northern Front rebels (one of the Carlist leaders), may surrender at any moment. (4) The "News" newspaper published a special issue stating that the government forces on the Guadarrama front behind the capital have begun to launch an offensive. (5) The newspaper also reported that the family members of Prime Minister Quiroga have returned to the capital from San Rafael City, passing through the rebel lines safely. (6) A train full of food arrived in the capital from the Eastern Province, and several truckloads of food arrived from Valencia City this morning. (7) The Ministry of the Interior issued a notice to all militia leaders that all members under the age of sixteen serving on the battlefield should be sent home. (Havas dispatch, 27th)

Navarre Rebel Commander Organizes Provisional National Defense Committee 67

Andaye, Southern France: It has been reported that General Gabanas, the rebel commander of Navarre province, has established a Provisional National Defense Committee in Burgos City, under the control of General Mola, the commander-in-chief of the Northern Front rebels. General Gabanas himself serves as the chairman of the committee, while Generals Zumalacárregui, Ponte, and Zúñiga serve as vice-chairmen. The committee exercises all political power, acting as a government. When a military dictatorship is established, it will hand over political power and send representatives to reside in foreign countries. The red and yellow colors are designated as the Spanish national flag, and the entire province of Navarre is now flying this flag. All other flags are prohibited. It is reported that the rebel forces in the province are currently advancing towards Pasajes City (on the coast of the Bay of Biscay) in the hope of gaining an outlet to the sea. If successful, traffic between Irún and Pamplona will be cut off, but the government forces are unlikely to concede, so a fierce battle is expected soon. Furthermore, the rebel forces in Loyola City near San Sebastian Port were surrounded and bombarded by government troops, but they broke through the siege and occupied the high ground around San Sebastian City. The sound of cannons is loud there, and a fierce battle is underway. (Havas dispatch, 26th)

Foreign Warships Rescue Nationals, U.S. Ambassador Leaves Spain 68

Madrid: A fleet of British and American warships are currently transporting foreign nationals out of Spain, providing assistance regardless of nationality. Today, the British warship "Calypso" arrived in Marseille with 260 foreign nationals from Barcelona. Most foreigners praised the extreme factions in Spain for their courteous treatment of foreigners. The only diplomatic incident to date was the shooting of a car from the Polish embassy in Madrid. The Polish government has lodged a formal protest with the Spanish government. The International Red Cross in Geneva has notified the Spanish Red Cross of its willingness to provide assistance, but the Spanish Red Cross has politely declined. (Reuters dispatch, 26th)

Andaye, Southern France: U.S. Ambassador to Spain Bowers was previously vacationing with his wife and daughters at a villa in Getaria, northern Spain. Due to the unstable situation and potential danger, Major Griffiths, the air attache of the U.S. Embassy in France, went to persuade him to leave the country. This morning, he and his family boarded the U.S. Coast Guard cutter "Cayuga" and left Spain. (Havas dispatch, 26th)

(Washington) Johnson, the Counselor of the American Embassy in Spain, reported to the State Department from San Sebastian today, stating that all American citizens there had boarded the customs patrol ship "Cayuga." Fighting in the suburbs is intense, and the rebels are gradually approaching. Johnson himself remains in Spain, temporarily staying at the summer villa of U.S. Ambassador Bowers, a few miles away. It is understood that the American citizens in Bilbao have also safely left the country, boarding the American warship Oklahoma. In the capital, the Third Secretary of the Embassy, Wendell, reported that they are trying to send American citizens to Valencia by rail. The government has ordered that no foreign nationals with formal passports be arrested, and that the military stop patrolling the streets. Police patrols must also wait until after 9:00 PM, and markets must reopen immediately to ensure that people do not run out of food. (National Telegraph, 26th)

Genoa, Italy: The postal ship "Princess Maria" arrived here this afternoon, carrying 1,600 foreign nationals from various parts of Spain who were evacuating to escape the conflict. The majority of these foreign nationals were from the United Kingdom, the United States, Germany, and Switzerland. (Havas dispatch, 26th)

(Berlin) The German "pocket battleship" Deutschland has arrived in San Sebastian today to protect German nationals there. Its sister ship, the "Admiral Scheer," will set sail for Barcelona in the next few days. (Reuters dispatch, 27th)

Eyewitness Account: Horrific Conditions in Barcelona - Churches Burned, Shops Looted, Corpses Litter Streets, Pervasive Stench 69

(Rome) 1,500 refugees arrived here from Barcelona, and many of them described the tragic events in Spain, which have caused concern in the Vatican. They claimed that hundreds of technicians and nuns have been killed. Many nuns were stripped naked and thrown into the streets. A total of 18 churches have been looted. Mobs forced technicians and nuns to set fire to a church and then shot them with machine guns. In the town of Cariaga, the guerrilla troops dug up corpses and lined them up against the walls of a church, doused them with oil, and burned them, forcing groups of nuns to watch. Another group of nuns was shot in front of the altar for refusing to set fire to a church. A female doctor secretly sent a letter from Barcelona to London, stating that rebels were firing from churches at those loyal to the government, so the churches and monasteries were burned. The rebels also fired upon a Red Cross vehicle, and she was sitting in the vehicle at the time. They also fired on unarmed civilians gathered outside the post office. (Reuters dispatch, 27th)

Madrid: According to a Reuters correspondent who recently arrived at Cerbère on the French-Spanish border from Barcelona, the historically valuable harbor there may face famine, even though it remains in the hands of those loyal to the government. The correspondent also described in detail the various tragedies in Barcelona, stating that the corpses of humans and animals were scattered throughout the streets, causing a pervasive stench that was unbearable. The correspondent also recounted that several rebel generals were hiding in a monastery, but were discovered by government troops and forced to surrender. However, the majority were killed, and none survived. One person had both feet cut off. All shops in Barcelona were looted. Many tram tracks have been destroyed. Except for a few churches and monasteries that have been converted into hospitals, all other places have been searched and robbed. Many anarchists set fire to the Church of Santa Ana, danced and rejoiced on the altar, and tore the image of Christ into pieces. The offices of the Italian shipping company have been looted and vandalized. As a result, the Governor of Catalonia, Companys, has ordered special protection for foreign property. According to the correspondent's observation, a 19-year-old girl led the newly formed Red Army, practicing with the men in a very agile manner. The British couple, Mr. and Mrs. Barton, arrived safely in Cerbère after experiencing terror in Barcelona. It is said that the Bartons were staying at the best hotel in the city. They were awakened by gunfire in the morning and discovered that the rebels were being attacked by government troops and had taken refuge in the hotel. Several rebels entered the Bartons' bedroom, told them to get up quickly, but did not allow them to change clothes. Then, the rebels fired back through the gaps in the windows until they were all shot dead. The Bartons lost all their money and luggage and arrived in Cerbère with only blood-stained clothes and leather shoes. According to a Reuters message from Lisbon, 80 nuns, one of whom was over 90 years old, have escaped from Vigo to Valpobus. Although they were tired from the journey, they insisted on first expressing their gratitude to God in the church of the monastery where they were staying before agreeing to rest.

(London) An Englishman arrived here today from Barcelona and claimed that almost all the cafes and grocery stores in the city had been robbed, and it was now very difficult to buy food and drinks. A Spaniard was hiding in the bedroom of an Englishman in a hotel, but was discovered by the crowd, who broke down the door and killed him in front of the Englishman. None of the churches in the city were intact. Many monks tried to escape in ordinary clothes, but were discovered and arrested because their boots were different from those of the general public. (Reuters dispatch, 26th)

France Strictly Maintains Neutrality in Spanish Civil War, Right-Wing Opposes Supplying Arms 70

(Paris) Right-wing newspapers have been relentlessly attacking the government recently because Spain has purchased weapons from France. However, according to a report in the Communist Party newspaper L'Humanité, the former Spanish ambassador to France, Quinones de Leon (who served as ambassador during the reign of the deposed King Alfonso), purchased airplanes and automobiles worth 20 million francs from the Renault factory on behalf of the Spanish Fascist Party. Quinones issued checks to pay for the goods, and Renault has received the payment. The right-wing newspapers are now saying that the Council of Ministers has decided to strictly maintain neutrality in the Spanish conflict, which is a commendable attitude. (Havas dispatch, 27th)

New Spanish Ambassador Departs for France to Assume Office 71

(Paris) The newly appointed Spanish Ambassador to Germany, Albornoz, departed from Madrid by plane at 8:45 this morning to assume his new post. He made stops in Barcelona and Lyon, France, and is expected to arrive here this afternoon. (Havas dispatch, 27th)

Brussels: The Chargé d'Affaires and Secretary of the Spanish Embassy in Brussels have both resigned. According to reports, the Chargé d'Affaires of the Spanish Embassy in France, the military attaché, and the Consuls General in Marseille and Bayonne resigned yesterday because the Spanish government purchased arms from France. (Havas dispatch, 26th)

Le Temps Discusses the Situation in Spain 72

(Paris) Le Temps recently published an article on the situation in Spain, expressing deep concern that the conflict in that country will have international repercussions. The article stated: "The situation in Spain is extremely confusing, and any attempt to interfere is extremely dangerous. The news coming out of that country is often contradictory. One side boasts of victory, while the other immediately dismisses it as lies. The location of real power is also unclear. Taking into account all the various circumstances, it appears that the power of the Republican government in Madrid extends only to a small part of the country, and even the extent to which it can exercise that power is limited by what the radicals will allow. These people volunteer to suppress the rebellion, and the government has no choice but to cooperate with them, so their strength is sufficient to control the government. The facts show that there are currently three power centers in Spain, which, although not yet clearly distinct, are undoubtedly independent. One is the government in Madrid, which is the current central government; the second is the government of the Autonomous Region of Catalonia, whose president, Companys, controls all the radical groups; and the third is the rebel party, which recently formed a provisional government in Burgos City, chaired by General Cabanellas. As for those engaged in the civil war in the provinces, they can be roughly divided into the Red and White parties, but each party is also divided into various factions with different tendencies. The Red Party includes radical trade unions and far-left Republicans, while the White Party is made up of moderate Republicans, royalists, and the remnants of the "Carlist" party. The leader of the Carlist party is Prince Carlos, the legitimate heir to the throne, who is eighty-six years old. People initially thought that the remnants had long been wiped out, but in fact, they still exist. The Red and White parties are engaged in mutual slaughter, which is inhumane. Regardless of who emerges victorious, Spain is suffering a great calamity, and the division of power and mutual hostility will inevitably continue. It will be extremely difficult to achieve political stability and return to normalcy. As for the international implications and crises, since the recent talks in London between France, Belgium, and Italy, a glimmer of hope has emerged for a general resolution of European problems. However, the problems related to the western Mediterranean are vital to the lifeblood of England and France, and Spain also has a direct interest. If measures are taken carelessly, Germany and Italy will immediately seize the opportunity to exploit the situation. As for France, it is all the more necessary to strictly maintain neutrality. To ensure the safety of our country in the Mediterranean and in our North African colony of Morocco, it is essential to maintain friendly relations with both France and Spain. France has always maintained cordial relations with both past and present governments of Spain, and regardless of how Spanish internal politics may change in the future, the friendly relations between the two countries must be maintained." (Havas dispatch, 26th)

Various Countries Jointly Request Protection of Embassies and Consulates 73

Madrid: The heads of diplomatic missions in Spain have jointly submitted a request to the government for full protection of the safety of their embassies, legations, and consulates, as well as freedom of postal and telegraphic communication with their home governments. They also requested that food supplies be guaranteed to prevent shortages. The Spanish government immediately expressed its agreement and said that it would provide protection to the best of its ability. In addition, the German Embassy in Spain, which originally had a summer office in San Sebastián, has now moved to Fuenterrabia. (Havas dispatch, 27th)

Belgian Socialist Party Sends Telegram to Spanish Government Expressing Sympathy 74

At the same time, the radio station in Pontevedra on the northwestern coast of Spain intercepted a telegram from the captain of the Spanish government warship "Libertad," stating that the ship was in a very dangerous situation due to a lack of fuel and water. President's Wife Serves Wounded Soldiers 76

Madrid: The wife of President Azaña organized a wounded soldiers' hospital at the Ophthalmic Medical College in the capital today, with 80 beds. It began operations today. (Havas dispatch, 27th)

Mediterranean Mutual Assistance Agreement, Britain Decides to Revoke, Simply to Please Italy and Induce it to Participate in Five-Power Conference 77

(London) The Cabinet Foreign Affairs Committee met this morning at 10 Downing Street, chaired by Prime Minister Baldwin, with Foreign Secretary Eden, First Lord of the Admiralty Hoare, and Home Secretary Simon in attendance. They discussed the situation in the House of Commons, which was scheduled to meet this afternoon, to prepare for it. It is generally believed that Foreign Secretary Eden will announce in the House of Commons that the British government has decided to revoke the Mediterranean Mutual Assistance Agreement. (Havas dispatch, 27th)

(London) In December of last year, when sanctions were imposed on Italy, Britain, based on Article 16 of the League of Nations Covenant, entered into mutual assistance agreements with countries along the Mediterranean coast (namely, France, Spain, Turkey, and Yugoslavia), providing guarantees to these countries that if they were attacked by Italy as a result of implementing sanctions, Britain would provide naval assistance. According to semi-official sources, Foreign Secretary Eden will announce this afternoon in the House of Commons that these guarantees should be revoked immediately. (It is reported that Italy demanded this as a condition for participating in the future Five-Power Conference.) Some sources also said that Britain may recognize Italy's new position in Abyssinia. Regarding this, the News Chronicle recently reported, "Anything that has already been seized in practice, even if legal ownership has not been obtained, is like building a mountain nine fathoms high and only lacking one basket of earth. The British government often accepts this principle and recognizes the missing basket of earth." The Morning Post reported that Foreign Secretary Eden's official announcement of the revocation of the Mediterranean Mutual Assistance Agreement would please Italy and induce that country to accept participation in the future Five-Power Conference. It is said that although sanctions have been lifted, the guarantees that Britain provided to the Mediterranean countries have been maintained because Italy still poses a threat in the Mediterranean. Italy has made assurances to the Mediterranean countries, stating that the alleged danger does not actually exist. (Havas dispatch, 27th)

Pan-Pacific Conference to Open in Mid-October in San Francisco; China-Japan Issue to be the Focus of Discussion 78

San Francisco—The Pacific International Academic Society is scheduled to hold a conference at Yosemite National Park from August 15th to 29th. The issue of Japanese aggression against China will be the focus of discussion. From all perspectives, this conference will be one of the most important since the establishment of the society. Each national delegation will consist of 25 to 35 members, including government officials and university professors. Participating countries include China, Japan, the Philippines, Canada, the United Kingdom, the Soviet Union, and the United States. Although the United Kingdom is not a Pacific nation, many of its territories are related to the Pacific, so it will also participate. The Soviet Union's decision to participate for the first time is also quite important. Since joining the League of Nations, the Soviet Union has begun to interact with European countries. Now, by joining the Pacific Academic Society, it will also meet with representatives from Pacific nations for the first time. The League of Nations will also send observers to attend the conference as usual. The League of Nations observer for this session has been designated as Lange Lennox, the current director of the League of Nations Paris branch and an expert on Far Eastern affairs. (National Telegram, 26th)

(Tokyo) Kenzo Oshima, Director of the Sumitomo Bank of Japan, departed for the United States today. Oshima's trip is to represent Japan at the upcoming Institute of Pacific Relations conference. (Hualian Telegram, 27th)

Japanese Fleet Maneuvers in Fujian Waters; Drills to Be Conducted Near Xiamen; Japanese Warships Freely Enter and Exit Xiamen Port 79

Xiamen Correspondence: Seventy-two warships of the Japanese First and Second Combined Fleets will arrive in Xiamen on August 1st. It is learned that the combined fleet, commanded by Admiral Sankichi Takahashi, departed from Sasebo, Japan, arrived in Taiwan on June 27th, and left Taiwan on July 1st for exercises in the South Seas Mandate Territory. It is currently returning and is scheduled to arrive in Xiamen on August 1st. The exercises in the Fujian and Taiwan waters will also begin on August 8th. Naval Attaché Suga from the Japanese Consulate General in Fuzhou is scheduled to travel from the provincial capital by ship on July 26th and arrive in Xiamen on the 27th to prepare for the reception. Suga stated in a speech in the provincial capital, "The joint maneuvers of the Japanese Combined Fleet in the waters of Taiwan and Fujian are purely for tactical training, with naval students practicing long-distance naval operations, and have no special significance. The fleet is scheduled to host Chinese officials and gentry in Xiamen on August 2nd, and return to Sasebo on the 5th to their original defense positions. The maneuvers will include the First and Second Fleets, the Third, Seventh, and Eighth Squadrons, the First and Second Submarine Squadrons, and the First and Second Mine Warfare Squadrons, totaling more than seventy warships, as well as three aviation squadrons." Furthermore, Taro Yamada, the Japanese Consul in Xiamen, told reporters in Xiamen on July 23rd, "The First and Second Combined Fleets have more than seventy warships. Their arrival in Xiamen has no specific mission and is the same nature as the fleet cruising near Qingdao. The fleet will be stationed in Xiamen for four or five days and will conduct offensive and defensive exercises near Xiamen. After the exercises, they will return to their home country for defense. The fleet is commanded by Admiral Takahashi, followed by fourteen squadron commanders with the rank of Rear Admiral or higher. The largest ship in the fleet is the Nagato battleship, with a displacement of 35,000 tons." It is noted that the Japanese Combined Fleet previously visited Xiamen in 1924, commanded by then-Prime Minister Keisuke Okada, but it was only a cruise visit without any exercises, and there were only about thirty warships. This is the second visit in twelve years. When they arrived in Taiwan at the end of last month, the First Fleet had forty ships, entering Kelung Port, and the Second Fleet had thirty-two ships, entering Kaohsiung Port. The entire fleet had 60,000 officers and soldiers. The essence of the Japanese Navy is all gathered here. Furthermore, the large-scale exercises from the South Seas Mandate Territory to the waters of Taiwan and Fujian are a major demonstration to the South Pacific, and its significance is not limited to our country. However, our country feels it especially deeply. With such a large fleet conducting offensive and defensive exercises near Xiamen, its emphasis on Xiamen is also evident. Moreover, Xiamen is an important naval port and a fortress area of our country. In the past, when foreign warships came to Xiamen, the consul of that country would notify the Xiamen Fortress Headquarters a few days in advance. Since 1934, when Japanese warships come to Xiamen, they do not notify in advance and enter the port at any time, and often leave the port at night, breaking the rule that the Xiamen Customs prohibits all ships from entering and leaving before 6:00 AM and after 6:00 PM every day. Also, on the 12th of last month, seven Japanese destroyers arrived in Xiamen and conducted night combat exercises in the waters outside Xiamen from the 14th, entering and leaving Xiamen Port at night. Since then, the 16th ship of the Japanese Fifth Mine Warfare Squadron has been conducting exercises between Taiwan, Shantou, and Xiamen for one or two weeks. Japanese warships come and go freely at night, entering and leaving frequently, as if it were their own military port. Recently, Li Shijia, commander of the Fuzhou Mawei Fortress, and Lin Guogeng, commander of the Xiamen Fortress, have jointly submitted a report to the Ministry of the Navy, requesting the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to negotiate with the Japanese ambassador so that Japanese warships will notify in advance when they come to Xiamen in the future. It is unknown what the outcome will be.

Yu Hanmou Arrives in Guangdong to Handle the Aftermath; Guangzhou Pacification Headquarters and the Fourth Route Army Headquarters Have Been Established; Military Restored to the Status Quo Before June 1st 80

Guangzhou Correspondence: Since Chen Jitang stepped down, the local military and police authorities have been maintaining public order. During this transition period, all groups and agencies are eager for the newly appointed Director of the Guangzhou Pacification Headquarters and Commander-in-Chief of the Fourth Route Army, Yu Hanmou, to arrive in the province as soon as possible to take charge of everything. Yu initially planned to arrive in the provincial capital on the 22nd, but it was delayed until the morning of the 23rd. That morning, Yu, along with Li Xuhuan and Chen Mianwu, secretaries of the Fourth Route Army Headquarters, Qian Dajun, director of the First Group of the Central Military Commission's Attendant's Office, Huang Zhenqiu, principal of the Aviation School, Tu Sizong, a division commander of the Central Army, and more than twenty others, traveled by three Central aircraft from Shaozhou to the province. More than twenty aircraft accompanied them. At 8:35 AM, they arrived at the Tianhe Airfield in Shipai, Guangzhou. In advance, troops from the First Division, military police, and police security teams were stationed around the airfield. Those who welcomed them from the military, political, party, and academic circles included Lin Yungai, Li Shuzong, Lin Shiqing, Fan Dexing, Zhang Zhiying, Chen Zhangfu, Huang Zhiwen, Huang Yanzhen, Zhang Guoyuan, Huang Renhuan, Zhou Jingzhen, Li Luchao, Deng Qingyang, Wen Zhongqi, Lu Kuangwen, Gan Jiehou, Zhang Da, Song Ziliang, Zou Lin, Tang Haian, and hundreds of others. Yu emerged from the No. 1201 aircraft and shook hands with each of the welcomers. He then took a car to the Yantang Military and Political School to rest. The Central personnel who came with him also went along. Later, Yu summoned the generals remaining in the province, including Lin Shiqing, Tang Haoqing, Li Shuzong, Miao Peinan, and dozens of others, at the military school and inquired in detail about the current situation in Guangdong Province. Li Shuzong reported on the public order in the provincial capital and the garrison situation of various armies. They dispersed at around 11:00 AM. On the same day, Yu issued a written statement, as follows: "This time, I flew to Nanjing to call for peace, to end the war and save the country, in order to implement the consistent principle of sincere unity and to face the national crisis together. In Nanjing, I met with several veteran gentlemen, received their guidance in person, and received the personal instructions of Chairman Chiang on all national salvation strategies. I immediately telegraphed to persuade the two Guangdong authorities to dispel their suspicions and resolve their disputes, to unite the national strength, and to resist the invaders together. Subsequently, I received a clear order from the Central Government, specially appointing me as the Director of the Guangzhou Pacification Headquarters and Commander-in-Chief of the Fourth Route Army. I could not refuse, so I telegraphed from Dayu to take office. I have spent half my life in the military and am content with simplicity. In this time of national crisis, I have long disregarded personal life, death, and safety. However, I cannot bear to see Guangdong, the source of the revolution, my hometown, fall into ruin, and the 30 million beloved fellow Cantonese people suffer eternal misfortune. Moreover, the revolutionary organizations that have struggled hard for more than ten years and the countless martyrs who have sacrificed, as well as the comrades-in-arms who have shared weal and woe for a long time, are deeply entrusted with my spirit and are closely related to me. How can I bear to see them all destroyed in one day? However, I believe that the interests of one individual are small, and the safety of the country and the nation is a great matter. Therefore, under the urging of the public, I resolutely accepted the order of the Central Government, telegraphed to return to the army, and cleaned up the Guangdong situation. I ask myself that I am straightforward in nature, and I have always adhered to the principles of impartiality, sincerity, kindness, and generosity towards people and things. I hope that the generals will continue to work together for many years and will be close and inseparable, and all will deeply understand the great righteousness and be able to entrust their hearts. At a time when the country is in trouble, we should share the same boat. Everything in the past can be put aside. We must all recognize the difficulties of the times, unite sincerely, and under the leadership of the Central Government's unified anti-aggression front, gather all our strength to defend the territory, pacify the local area, and seek a way out for the country and the nation, in order to repay the trust of the Party and the country and the hopes of the Cantonese people, and to fulfill the duty of a soldier. I have always been in awe of the clear warning that soldiers should not interfere in politics and harm the country. Today, I bear a heavy responsibility and feel even more frightened. In order to eliminate the bad habits of the past, I deeply wish to take the lead by example, not to ask about politics, and to focus on training the military for the use of the country. In the military aspect, we should first restore the status quo before June 1st, so that the hearts of the people in Guangdong can quickly stabilize. At a time when the country is poor and the people are impoverished, and the economy is in a state of recession, we should broaden our minds and vision and take the overall national strength and the lives of the entire people as the premise. I have always hoped to bring fewer soldiers, so that I can reduce one point of sin, which is to reduce one point of burden on the people and cultivate one point of vitality in the local area. Therefore, I strongly advocate that the financial affairs of this province should be the responsibility of the Central Government for consolidation, in order to conform to the original intention of complete and genuine unification. All people in Guangdong should clearly understand the Central Government's painstaking efforts this time and its determination to maintain the integrity of Guangdong and to prioritize the local people. We should not have private opinions and arbitrarily divide our territories. The Central Government will certainly be able to take into account the overall financial plan of the country and coordinate everything. We only need to help with consolidation in the spirit of consistent trust and cooperation from top to bottom, so that we can achieve full effect as soon as possible, to relieve the people's difficulties and to build national defense. This is the only way for the Cantonese people to turn danger into safety and the only way to save the situation. Our compatriots' revolutionary enthusiasm has long been known at home and abroad. At this critical moment of life and death, I believe that we can clearly understand the international environment, unite together, assist the government, strive to improve, jointly protect the territory, and forever maintain the reputation of the source of the revolution. I have always loved the words "practical" and "hardworking" the most, and I often use them to encourage myself, and I dare to use them to encourage my 30 million Cantonese elders, brothers, sisters, and aunts, to work together to create a new and self-reliant Guangdong."

After Yu arrived in the province, all sectors expressed their welcome. Yu also issued an announcement to reassure the people, exhorting the people to maintain peace and pacify the local area. He also consulted on military and local affairs for days in order to start consolidation. In order to pacify the local area and consolidate the military and government, the Guangzhou Pacification Commission Office was established as the highest authority. The former First Army Group Headquarters was changed to the Pacification Headquarters. The headquarters was divided into six sections: Staff, Secretarial, Adjutant, Military Supplies, Military Medicine, and Military Law, each with a Major General as the section chief, and a Lieutenant General as the Chief of Staff. The Fourth Route Army Headquarters was located at the former Mingde Society site on Nonglin Road in Dongshan. The headquarters was divided into Staff, Secretariat, Adjutant, Military Law, Military Medicine, Logistics, Political Training, and Military Reclamation sections. Luo Zicai was appointed as the Chief of the Staff Section, Li Xuhuan as the Chief of the Secretariat Section, Ma Binghong as the Chief of the Logistics Section, Zhang Jian as the Chief of the Military Medicine Section, and Xu Jingtang as the Chief of Staff.

The 123rd Divisions of Yu's Fourth Route Army have been transported to the province for days. The First Division under Li Zhen is stationed in the suburbs of the provincial capital, the Second Division is stationed along the Guangzhou-Sanshui Road, and the Third Division is stationed in the northern suburbs of the provincial capital, along the Yuehan Road to Xinjie. The divisions of the Second Army are stationed in the Xiaobei River and Xijiang Qing, and the Third Army is still stationed in the counties of Huizhou. The Fourth Army is stationed in Xingning, Fengshun, and Meixian. The defense areas of each army will not be adjusted in the short term. (July 24th)

Smuggling in North China Slows Down Slightly; Customs Anti-Smuggling Efforts Intensified; Smuggled Goods to the South Have Disappeared 81

Tianjin Correspondence: Smuggled goods transported from Tianjin to the south have been cut off since the night of the 21st. This situation is partly due to the accumulation and sluggish sales of smuggled goods in areas south of Jinan, and partly because the Tianjin Main Station was detained by the Customs on the night of the 21st with a batch of smuggled goods heading south. The Ronin feared losses and automatically stopped transportation. On the night of the 22nd, although dozens of Ronin transported about 40 loads of yarn, sugar, and rayon to the East Railway Station, they feared that the Customs would detain them, so they transported them back to the Japanese Concession without waiting to load them onto the train. From mid-May, when the Ronin began to forcibly occupy the Jinpu Railway to go south, to a certain day, it lasted for more than seventy days. The Jinpu Railway estimates that the loss of reduced passenger transport due to ticket refunds is about 1,500 yuan per day. The loss of freight costs is more than 4,000 yuan. In the past seven weeks, the total loss reached more than 40 million yuan, and the indirect losses are not included. Regarding the smuggled goods seized on the 21st, the Japanese Consul-General in Tianjin, at the request of the Ronin Trade Association, sent Commercial Vice-Consul Nagai to the Customs to visit Chief Tax Inspector Xu Liya to request their return. Xu refused, and Nagai did not insist on any claims and left. Due to the stricter enforcement of anti-smuggling efforts in recent days, the sea patrols are also operating normally. The Guanghao gunboat, which is stationed in Tanggu, is still cruising in Qikou and Dagu. As a result, the number of smuggling ships in this area has decreased. However, sailboats and small steamers are still constantly transporting goods from the Tuohekou area. It is learned that the Tianjin Customs has issued a vernacular notice to strictly block the import and export of smuggled goods, stating, "All citizens of the Republic of China should rise up to help the country and eliminate smuggling merchants. If you hear any news about smuggling merchants, hurry to report to the Customs area. After capturing the smuggled goods ship, the reporter will receive a reward. For example, if the auction is 10,000 yuan, 5,000 yuan will be given as a reward. If you have accurate information, you can tell the Tax Officer, Deputy Tax Officer, Inspector General, Deputy Inspector General, Head of the Customs Branch Office, or Captain of the Patrol Boat in person. However, the reporter must also keep the secret strictly." Since the posting of this notice, smugglers have become more cautious and no longer rampant. This is also one of the reasons.

According to statistics for July to date, only 15,000 packages of smuggled yarn and sugar have been transported from Tianjin to the south. Due to difficulties in transportation earlier and interception by the Customs recently, there are currently more than 300,000 packages stockpiled in the Tianjin Japanese Concession, and more than 400,000 packages stockpiled in Dalian. In the past three months, the sales volume of yarn and sugar has been 56,000 packages per month, so based on the current stockpile, it will take at least half a year to sell them all. If the monthly sales are 30,000 packages, it may take no less than ten months to clear them all. Moreover, the prices are falling sharply. In this one item alone, the Ronin and smugglers have lost more than one million yuan in one week. From the Japanese perspective, smuggling is coming to an end. Its sales cannot continue to be rampant as they are now, and prices can only plummet and cannot rise. The losses of major Japanese industries and businesses are a hundred times greater than the private profits made by a few Ronin. Moreover, due to smuggling, domestic prices in Japan have fallen sharply, and commerce and industry cannot be maintained. It would be better to help crack down on smuggling so that large industries and businesses can trade legally. Therefore, they have recently shown remorse and are no longer supporting it. However, they do not want to stop there. They intend to use the crackdown as a bargaining chip. If we agree to slightly reduce tariffs, they will help ban smuggling. There is no doubt about it. (26th)

Songjiang: Drowning While Practicing Swimming 82

Zhang Yundiao, a young man in his early twenties, a staff member of the county government's deed tax office, recently enjoyed learning to swim. Last Friday, he did not attend the morning exercise, which was quite strange to his colleagues. However, he stayed overnight at the county government, so his family did not find it strange. The colleagues at the county government thought he had returned home, so they also did not find it strange. On a certain evening, a naked male corpse was found in the inner city river behind the Catholic Church. After passing the word around, someone finally identified it as Zhang Yundiao. His body was swollen and his face was blurred. After notifying his family, they reported to the prosecutor's office to come for an inspection. It was heard that there were no signs of injury. It was likely that he had lost his footing while practicing swimming and drowned. However, it was quite strange that he was completely naked. His father, Zhang Polang, was very saddened when he heard the news.

Suzhou: Arrests in Meat Merchant Dispute 83

The meat industry in Suzhou believes that since they have already paid the slaughter tax, they should not have to pay the business tax again. They have repeatedly argued, but have not been granted permission by the authorities. However, the industry is still arguing. The Wu County Business Tax Bureau believes that the industry intends to resist taxes, so it sent a letter to the county government requesting the arrest and detention of Jiang Kunqing from the Lao Zhenxing partnership and Chen Maoda from the Chen Sanzhen partnership. As a result, the industry was panicked and immediately convened a general meeting, appointing Zhang Zhiming, Xu Kunquan, Ni Shenan, and nine others as representatives to visit Chairman Cheng of the County Chamber of Commerce on the 27th, requesting that the bureau be urged to release the arrested Jiang and Chen and to find ways to guarantee their safety. Chairman Cheng then negotiated with the bureau, but regarding the business tax issue, the bureau insisted on collecting taxes in accordance with regulations. They are currently discussing solutions.

"Sucking Essence" Case to Be Indicted 84

Coincidentally, the cases of Wu Yifei of Shantang Street and Lu Fuming of Xumenwai sucking the essence of apprentices have been investigated by the District Prosecutor's Office, which has detained Wu and Lu for investigation. The victims, Li Xiangxiang and others, were summoned and interrogated separately, and the case has been clarified. An indictment will be filed within days. Wu Yifei has firmly requested the District Prosecutor's Office to send the victims to the Institute of Forensic Medicine for examination to determine whether his injuries were caused by sucking essence. Lu Fuming has entrusted someone to reconcile with the victim.

Full Traffic on the Su-Fu Highway 85

Since Chen Qinshi of Wuxing took over the long-distance buses on the Su-Jia-Hu Highway, he has widened and repaired the road surface between Pingwang and Huzhou, which has been completed. A simple opening ceremony will be held on August 1st. The Su-Mu section of the Su-Fu Highway has long been completed and opened to traffic. The highway between Mu and Guangfu has also been completed and will be fully opened to traffic on September 1st.

Kunshan: Building the Kun-Qing County Road 86

The route of the county road connecting this county to Qingpu has long been surveyed. The road connects Qingpu and Songjiang to the south, and Shanghai to the southeast, which is an important area for Su-Song defense. However, due to financial difficulties, construction has not yet started. It is learned that the county government will work with the Qingpu County Government to conduct a detailed survey again in order to start construction as soon as possible. In addition to using the road construction tax donated by the two counties, a small amount will be requested from the province for subsidies.

Wuxi: Discussing Jiangsu and Zhejiang Silkworm Seeds 87

The Silkworm Seed Industry Association of this county held a membership meeting yesterday and resolved: (1) The original autumn varieties Zhugui, Hangui, and Hua 5 were made in the spring and submitted to the Management Committee for approval to avoid unnecessary sacrifices. (2) The model area improvement institutes and various planting sites should be clearly explained to the Management Committee. (3) The trial site forwarded the association's telegram stating that silkworm seeds exported from this county to Zhejiang that do not meet 1,000 sheets must be supplemented to 1,000 sheets, otherwise they will be eliminated. The association will send a list by telegram to reply. (4) The Improvement Association will be asked to subsidize the seed money. The association's regulations stipulate that the autumn production volume should not be less than 50% of the spring production volume. The association will be responsible for purchasing 1.35 million spring seeds next spring. (5) The silkworm seeds exported from this county to other provinces will be discussed by Zhu Ruifang, Miao Shoujun, and Lu Zirong, and the results will be notified to each site. (6) All spring and autumn made spring seeds at each site in this county should be reported to the association after the autumn production is completed so that methods can be devised for comprehensive export at any time. It is heard that Jiangsu Province will produce a net total of 1.24 million sheets of autumn seeds this year. Jiangsu Province will allocate 800,000 sheets, and the remaining 440,000 sheets will be sold to Zhejiang Province. The female silkworm farming instructors in each district of this county will depart on August 5th to provide guidance.

Changshu: Grain Tax Embezzlement Case Expanding 88

The embezzlement case discovered by the County Government's Grain Collection Office has attracted attention from all parties. It has long been known that the collection office is rife with corruption. Although the Provincial Committee and others have come to Changshu to investigate thoroughly, they have ultimately failed to discover anything because of the internal unity. The current discovery involves Zhou Ruixin forging grain slips in the past, and now discovering the embezzlement of inventory slips. It is heard that this situation is entirely due to internal cracks. The currently detained Zhou Ruixin is the cousin of Zhou Zhiqing, the director of the West Counter. When it was first discovered, it was intended to be covered up. However, Deputy Director Gu Yansheng believed that this was the best opportunity for promotion, so he directly informed the head of the Second Section and had Zhou arrested and detained. Because Zhou, as the perpetrator, is not the only one involved, all the officers, big and small, on the counter have embezzled thousands of yuan, or at least hundreds of yuan. Now, they are sacrificing one person and intend to make everything public. At this point, everyone is terrified and has submitted their resignations, resulting in a stalemate. Therefore, in recent days, the relevant parties have been doing their best to run around and dredge the situation, hoping to bail out Zhou Ruixin, the forger of grain slips, first to silence him, so that the situation will not expand. However, according to the county magistrate, he is determined to thoroughly clarify the situation in order to resolve the long-standing and unbreakable accumulated malpractices in the grain tax.

Opera House Vandalized 89

The Meiyuan Bookstore recently opened in North Zhao Alley has now been converted into an opera house. However, on the night of the 26th, soldiers from the 10th Security Brigade went to watch the opera and had an argument over the purchase of tickets. Then, when the show ended, suddenly thirty to fifty soldiers rushed into the opera house and vandalized it. The audience fled in disorder. As a result, many tables, chairs, teapots, and cups were damaged. The manager of the opera house reported to the brigade headquarters. The next morning, the brigade headquarters identified six of the perpetrators and sent them to the Public Security Bureau for investigation. All losses will be compensated by Huang Renbo, the commander of the company.

Changzhou: Major Robbery Case Solved, Loot and Suspect Recovered 90

Duan Guangrong, a resident of East Zhijie in Wu Township, held a wedding ceremony for his daughter, Mrs. Yu, on the 7th of this month at the Dacheng Hotel. However, when the bride was washing her face, the jewelry box she brought with her suddenly disappeared, containing gold bracelets and other jewelry worth more than 500 yuan. The Duan family immediately reported the case to the Public Security Bureau's First Branch for investigation and took the matchmaker, Mrs. Ding Sun, to the bureau for questioning. As a result, there were no leads. The Duan family then sent people to various pawnshops to inquire for days. On the 25th, two gold bracelets were found at the Jiheng Pawnshop, so they registered the loss and redeemed them. Then, on the 26th, a remaining ring was found at the Deyuan Pawnshop. When they went to register the loss, Feng Xiaomazi, a man from Haizhou living in Jianju Lane, happened to be holding a ticket to redeem the gold ring. Duan Guangrong questioned him about the source, but Feng could not answer. He immediately called the police and transferred Feng to the First Branch of the Public Security Bureau. They then searched his home. Feng's mother knew that things were not good and tried to throw the jewelry into the toilet, but it was found by the police in her stocking. Feng's mother, Chen, and others were taken to the bureau. After Duan Guangrong checked the items, three items, including the lock plate, were missing. Feng Xiaomazi confessed that they were pawned in Danyang. It was also stated that a wallet lost by a Li from the Dacheng Hotel was also stolen by him.

Nantong: Request to Reduce Land Tax Surcharges 91

Sun Songtao and others from the county believe that the land tax surcharges have been increasing every year since 1927. Last year, it reached 16 yuan per mu. The rental income of landowners is not enough to pay the grain tax. Now that the new budget has been established, they believe that there are too many heavy taxes and have specially requested the provincial capital to review and reduce them.

Pinghu: Where Do So Many Floating Corpses Come From? 92

In the waters off the Longwang Temple in Zhapu, many corpses have been floating up for days, including men, women, old, and young, as well as fashionable young girls. The left breast seems to have been bitten off by a giant fish. It is suspected that they are the family members of officials involved in the Daishan salt case. As of yesterday, twelve bodies have been found, but no one has come forward to collect them.

The Entire Town Sacrifices Itself, Bare-Chested 93

The Xincang District Office recently dispatched officers to interfere with citizens going bare-chested. On the 23rd, a certain sauce garden initiated resistance, willing to sacrifice the entire town's commerce, vowing to fight for survival bare-chested. Agreement having been reached, a market strike was immediately initiated. Pawnshops also joined the battle, resulting in the poor having no money to pawn for a time, all bitterly scolding the authorities. Yesterday, the county government and county chamber of commerce sent people to persuade them, but to no avail. Today, the county party headquarters sent personnel to investigate. This morning, a phone call was made to inquire, but there was still no news of the market reopening.

Yangzhou: Early Rice with Double Ears at Donghui 94

Donghui, in the Qili Xu area of Fanchuan Township, Jiangdu County, is backed by mountains and faces a river, spanning over forty li in circumference. The farmland only grows autumn rice, and the harvests are always abundant. This year, the seedlings were transplanted in April and are now all yellowing and ripening. The early rice can be harvested in ten days. This phenomenon has never occurred in previous years. This year, several families, including Li Tiancai and Wang Juxing, due to proper fertilization, have rice ears with two branches, which the entire township regards as an auspicious sign.

Bengbu: Two Notorious Bandits Arrested and Escorted to Xu 95

Han Fei and Hu Benxun, nicknamed Hu Mazi, from northern Jiangsu, have been robbing and kidnapping in the Xu area for some time, committing numerous crimes. In the past week, they gathered a gang of bandits to rob the No. 117 road worker's house of the fifth section of the Jin-Pei Railway. Afterward, they fled to the Jiulonggang area of the Huainan mining district, about a hundred li from Bengbu, to hide. The Xuzhou police department received a confidential report and dispatched seven police officers to arrest them. Hu Benxun and Hu Mazi were captured in Jiulonggang. On the evening of the 25th, they were escorted to Bengbu and then transported by express train to the Xuzhou Garrison Headquarters for legal proceedings.

Jiangyin: Robbery at the Eastern Outer Road Intersection 96

Zhang Jiayu, company commander of the 4th company of the 2nd battalion of the garrison, resides at No. 9, 6th Jia, 3rd Bao, Wending Town, outside the east gate. At about 1:00 AM on the 26th, his wife, Ms. Mou, was at home when three thugs broke in through the roof and stole over 230 yuan in legal tender. Zhang's wife was stabbed by the thugs, but fortunately, she is not in life-threatening danger. The injured person has been sent to the Gospel Hospital for treatment. The town mayor has reported the incident to the Public Security Bureau for investigation.

Haizhou: Establishing Xuzhou-Haizhou Telephone Line 97

The Jiangsu Provincial Long-Distance Telephone Exchange has recently dispatched engineer Chen, along with an engineering team, to Haizhou to establish a long-distance telephone line between Xuzhou and Haizhou, aiming to develop communications in northern Jiangsu. After arriving in the county, Engineer Chen immediately consulted with Director Fan of the County Government Construction Department to discuss all installation procedures.
