Sports News

World Games to Open Soon Athletes Arriving in Germany One After Another Also Arriving: Mexico, Sweden, and Six Other Countries Marathon Winner to Receive Ancient Helmet 176

(Kuomintang News Agency, Berlin, July 26) World Games athletes are now arriving here in a steady stream. Several countries have sent advance teams, with the remainder to follow. Those officially welcomed today included teams from Mexico, Galatia, Sweden, Greece, and Lithuania.

At 6:00 PM, 127 Canadian athletes arrived here by special train from Berlin. In addition to official personnel, the British Consul General and others welcomed them at the station. Among them were 23 female athletes.

Ancient Helmet Prize Most Valuable

(Kuomintang News Agency, Berlin, July 26) The most unique and valuable prize at this World Games is the one awarded to the marathon winner. This prize is an ancient helmet, recently discovered near ancient Olympia. It is believed to be from the 6th century BC. Although it has been around for a long time, the helmet is still well preserved. According to experts, this helmet is of great value to ancient studies. This helmet is a gift from the director of a Greek newspaper, so a silver shield will be engraved with a commemorative inscription inside the helmet.

Chinese Martial Arts Team Trains Day and Night

(Kuomintang, Berlin, July 27) In addition to learning German day and night, the Chinese World Games martial arts team is working hard in training. The coach has instructed all athletes to get up at 6:00 AM every morning and rest at 10:00 PM in the evening. According to the coach, the training results of the athletes are extremely satisfactory.

World Games Torch Passes Through Bulgaria to Yugoslavia Church Bells Ring in Unison Before Bulgarian Prime Minister's Office Reaches Disputed Area Between Two Countries After 23 Hours 177

(Kuomintang News Agency, Sofia, July 36) The World Games torch, carried from ancient Olympia to Berlin, arrived here this morning. It has been widely welcomed and celebrated by the public here, as in other places. Before dawn today, the torch bearers reached the Catholic church in front of the Prime Minister's Office. An altar was built in front of the church, and a lamp was specially set up on the altar to light the torch. The Prime Minister led all cabinet members to wait respectfully on the scene. When the torch arrived, the Mayor of Sofia lit the lamp on the altar, and then the church bells rang in unison. Airplanes circled in the sky to celebrate. After the military band played the Bulgarian national anthem, a brief religious ceremony was held, and another person held the torch and headed towards the Yugoslav border.

(Kuomintang News Agency, Yugoslav Capital, July 26) At 1:05 AM this morning, the World Games torch arrived at Saribud City, on the border between Bulgaria and Yugoslavia. It took a total of 23 hours to pass through the Bulgarian border. Saribud is located in the mountains. Although the time was very inconvenient, the residents of the border between the two countries still gathered there to watch the torch enter the Yugoslav border. This place has historically been a point of contention between Bulgaria and Yugoslavia, and armed conflicts have been frequent. However, the atmosphere of harmony today is a major positive reversal. After various ceremonies, the Bulgarian runner handed the torch to the Yugoslav runner, who then set off towards Nas. He arrived at his destination at 8:30 this morning. At 9:25 tonight, the torch will reach Kragujevac. At 1:30 AM on the 26th, it will reach Osovna. The remains of Alexander I, the "Unifier of Yugoslavia," who was assassinated in Marseille in 1934, are buried there. When the runner arrives at Ovrena, he will light the eternal flame in front of the tomb of Alexander I and observe a minute of silence. After this, King Peter II of Yugoslavia will light the torch and run one kilometer.

(Kuomintang News Agency, Yugoslav Capital, July 27) The World Games artillery arrived here at 9:20 this morning. A large group of farmers had been waiting outside the city for a long time, and they welcomed its arrival and held a celebration ceremony.

World Games Athletes Accompanying Expedition (3rd Letter, Continued from Yesterday) Sent by Central News Agency Correspondent Feng Youzhen (10) (9) Basketball Team Slightly Wins Over New Federation

Yesterday (2nd) afternoon at 4:00 PM, the basketball team played an unofficial friendly match with the Singapore Combined Team. Originally, our athletes were very tired in body and spirit after six or seven days of sailing. Several of them could barely eat, and a match was absolutely impossible. However, the overseas Chinese in Singapore were very eager to have a friendly match. They had already gathered the best players from each team, trained them, and sold tickets without even seeking our consent (50 cents each, equivalent to one yuan in national currency). Many people from various cities on the Malay Peninsula came to see this match. After the ship docked, representatives from various organizations requested a match after the public banquet. Everyone pushed the responsibility onto Coach Dong Shouyi, who had no choice but to agree. At 3:30 PM, the basketball court in the Great World was already packed. The martial arts team first performed, and the program was very exciting, winning a lot of applause from the overseas Chinese. At 3:45 PM, the athletes entered the arena to stretch their muscles and bones. They first divided into two teams to perform for six minutes. Team A was Wang Yuzeng, Mou Zuoyun, Wang Hongbin, Li Shaokang, and Wang Nanzhen. Team B was Liu Qicheng, Feng Nianhua, Xu Zhaoxiong, Liu Yunzhang, and Cai Yanxiong. As a result, Team A won 8 to 2. At 4:00 PM, the athletes and the New Federation Team lined up for battle. The athletes sent out their most elite Team A, with three forwards darting in and out of the enemy's camp as if they were in no-man's land. In less than two minutes, they scored four goals. When the athletes scored 12 points, the New Federation only scored one. The excitement of the performance left the overseas Chinese stunned. Later, the athletes took turns replacing team members, and their spirits were not as excited as at the beginning. They politely let the New Federation Team slowly catch up. After playing for 30 minutes non-stop, the athletes won slightly by a score of 28 to 25. Everyone rushed back to the ship, leaving Singapore amidst the enthusiastic farewells of the overseas Chinese. (Recorded July 3rd)

(2) (10) Sailing in the Indian Ocean

After leaving Singapore, the ship moved forward in the Strait of Malacca. It was a night in the middle of the lunar month, and a bright moon illuminated the sky. Fleeting clouds streaked like arrows, and a silver light reflected on the calm sea surface, evoking an indescribable beauty. We lay on deck in wicker chairs, intoxicated in the embrace of nature, truly feeling refreshed and almost feeling like ascending to heaven.

The next morning, the sun reappeared. The shores of the Strait of Malacca were lush with trees, and the scenery was very beautiful. Everyone felt very comfortable with this kind of sea travel. At 10:00 AM, the discussion committee invited Ms. Huang Liming to give a lecture on European etiquette in the second-class smoking room. Many people went to listen.

In the evening, the ship had passed through the Strait of Malacca and was sailing in the Indian Ocean. This Indian Ocean, known for its wind and waves, had not yet shown its most ferocious form, but the ship's body was already swaying up and down, far less comfortable and stable than when sailing in the Strait of Malacca. Those who were afraid of seasickness hid in their cabins and lay down. At dinner, there were many empty seats in the dining room. At 9:00 PM, the entertainment committee held an entertainment party on the first-class deck. All Chinese and foreign passengers on the ship were invited to participate. A total of 300 people attended. Chairman Shen Siliang sang the party song and gave an opening speech. Then, he invited the captain to give a brief speech, and then the entertainment program began. First, Wang Huaiqi and Jiang Zhende collaborated to perform a skit of a midget giving a speech, followed by a martial arts performance. Although they could not fully demonstrate their skills due to the low cabin and the ship's shaking, each program was very exciting, winning thunderous applause. Many foreign passengers especially praised it. Qu Lianyuan and Zheng Huaixian performed a skit of sparring. As a result, Ms. Qu's elbows were bruised in several places, and Strongman Zheng also had several red marks, showing how seriously they performed. Over the past two days (4th and 5th), the wind and waves have become more and more ferocious. The rising and falling wave peaks produced milky white foam, which hit the ship's body, splashing water one or two dozen feet high. The sea breeze made a tiger-like roar, which was frightening. The ship's body swayed up and down and left and right as if in rhythm, making many people dizzy. The number of people eating decreased even further. Even those who could support themselves to walk to the dining room only did so perfunctorily. Mr. Chu Anping of the Central Daily News, who was in the same room and at the same table as me, lay in bed for two days, unable to leave the bed even one step. Mr. Luo Gusun of the International Photography Agency, who had the capacity of a giant, only shook his head and sighed at the dishes.

Today (5th) at 10:00 AM, the Fellowship Association held its first meeting in the second-class smoking room. Only compatriots on the ship were allowed to participate. Because the wind and waves were too strong, only seventy or eighty people attended. Chairman Shen Siliang gave a speech, followed by speeches by Jiang Yong, president of the Fellowship Association, and Pan Huaguo, deputy military attaché stationed in Germany. Then, everyone introduced themselves by name and surname to show their introduction. Deng Bingling, the China Travel Service agent accompanying the ship, also provided tea and refreshments, and everyone dispersed in joy. It is planned to hold another meeting before leaving the ship, and perhaps more people can participate at that time.

The Xiangqi (Elephant Chess) Championship has reached the final stage. The two gentlemen who won the right to the final are Qian Yiqin and Wu Demao. The two gentlemen are truly evenly matched, fighting fiercely for several rounds without a winner. As a result, they ended up splitting the championship. I met General Qian in the first week and was defeated. However, the tension of the situation could not be compared even to the final week. I only managed to "eat" after one win and one loss, which was somewhat comforting.

The ship is scheduled to arrive in Colombo, the capital of Ceylon, at 1:00 PM tomorrow (6th), completing a voyage of 1,576 nautical miles. There will probably be a six or seven-hour stopover. Everyone hopes that time will pass quickly, and perhaps the extremely tired spirits and bodies can recover somewhat at that time. (Recorded July 5th, sent from Colombo July 6th) (End)

Fifth International Swimming Competition Four Units Including China and Japan Compete Various Countries' Representatives Meeting Held Yesterday Resolved Eight Important Items Chinese Team's Preliminary Registration Deadline is August 2nd, Preliminary Competition on the 4th 179

After the West China Youth Association (WCYA) informally decided the holding of the 5th Quadrennial International Swimming Championship on the evenings of the 8th and 9th of next month, the Shanghai International Swimming Committee, which is in charge of the competition, held its first official representatives meeting at the WCYA on Jing'an Temple Road yesterday at 5:30 PM, presided over by Chairman Huxley. The meeting decided the scoring method, officials, competition events, and accepted the Chinese team's proposal to include water polo and diving as non-scoring exhibition events. Therefore, the Chinese team has very high hopes for winning the championship this year. Furthermore, the China National Amateur Athletic Federation (CNAAF) also held a meeting of the Chinese Swimming Committee yesterday afternoon at the Dengtomo Hotel to prepare for the Chinese team's participation in the competition. The meeting decided on the date of the preliminary competition, participating events, and registration location. The reporter has recorded the details as follows:

Meeting of Representatives from Various Countries

The International Swimming Committee held an official meeting of representatives from various countries at the West China Youth Association at 5:30 PM yesterday afternoon. Attendees included Huxley, Blatter, Brooks, Ling Xitao, Wang Fudan, Yu Binqi, Yamamoto, Hirota, Huegena, Brown, chaired by Blatter and recorded by Yu Binqi. The following resolutions were made: (1) The participating units in the 5th International Swimming Championship are the Chinese team, the British-American combined team, the Japanese team, and the Federal team. (2) The competition will be held on the evenings of August 8th and 9th at 8:30 PM at the Municipal Swimming Pool. (3) The competition events include a total of ten events. Water polo will have a separate championship, adopting an elimination system. Synchronized swimming and the women's 150-meter three-style relay will be exhibition events and will not be scored. (4) The scoring method for both individual and relay events will be 5-3-1. (5) All affairs will be handled by the Municipal Sports Field. The order of events and advertisements will be the responsibility of the International Swimming Committee. (6) Swimmers must wear full swimsuits. (7) Officials were appointed (see below). (8) The order of events for the two days was arranged (see below). (Note: The teams participating in the water polo championship are China, Britain, America, and the Federal team. Japan will not participate.)

Officials

Educational News

Municipal Elementary Schools Hire Teachers - Preferably Employ Graduates of Municipal Normal Schools - If Transfer is Needed, Must First Submit to the Bureau for Approval - Education Bureau Issued an Order to All Elementary Schools to Comply 189

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau issued an order to all municipal elementary schools, stating, "Upon investigation, when municipal elementary schools in this city hire teachers, they should preferentially employ graduates from the municipal Xinlu Normal School and the normal departments of Wuben Girls' High School and Jingye High School in this city. Those who are already employed as teachers and staff should not be arbitrarily replaced by the schools if their teaching is still good. This has already been strictly ordered for compliance in previous cases. Now, according to a report from the Xinlu Normal School Alumni Association, since the members of this association graduated from their alma mater, there are sixty to seventy people who have been able to serve in this city. If it were not for your care and support, how could this be achieved? Therefore, the members of this association, in addition to being deeply grateful, sincerely wish to work wholeheartedly and diligently under your leadership, without complaint, to fulfill their duties and seek to develop education in this city and contribute to your great kindness. As for the protection of the positions of the members of this association, you first established the regulations for the service of graduates from municipal normal schools, and then issued a unified order to all schools to preferentially employ graduates from municipal normal schools, and repeatedly instructed the schools not to arbitrarily change the principals who graduated from municipal normal schools. Your concern and protection for the members of this association can be said to be utmost. However, a small number of school principals ignore your instructions regarding the protection of the positions of the members of this association, without attaching importance to preferential employment, and those who have been arbitrarily changed after being employed have experienced anxiety over the years and cannot settle into their positions, merely feeling regret for not being able to fulfill their ambitions, resentment for not being able to promote education, and嘆 for not being able to repay your kindness, daring to express the greatest sincerity, without presuming to request your support for the members of this association, strictly ordering all schools to preferentially employ graduates from the municipal normal schools in this city, and those who have already been employed must not be changed or suspended without reason. If the already employed graduates from municipal normal schools have committed major errors, the points of error must be submitted to you in detail, requesting your review and compliance. Without your order, they must not be rashly changed or suspended. In this way, the members of this association can work with peace of mind and strive to develop education in this city under the protection, following you to complete the mission that the members of this association should bear." Accordingly, all graduates from the normal school or the normal departments of the municipal Wuben Girls' High School and Jingye High School who were originally hired by the schools should be protected. If a transfer is needed, the principals of the schools should be responsible for reporting their service records in detail for a decision. As the appointment period for the first semester of the 25th academic year is approaching, if the schools need to rehire or add teachers, they should still preferentially employ graduates from the municipal normal school and the normal department, otherwise, the appointment will not be approved. In addition to instructing them to be informed, the schools are hereby ordered to comply with this order. Be sure to do so.

Zhejiang Province's 25th Year - Central Work of Educational Facilities - Dedication to Teacher Training and Promotion of Compulsory Education - Training Youth Corps and Reorganizing County Educational Funds and Properties 193

(Hangzhou Correspondence) In order to make education at all levels suitable for the spirit of the Three Principles of the People and to promote the mission of national rejuvenation, the Zhejiang Provincial Department of Education has focused on the fundamental issues of national survival in recent years in its administrative facilities. For example, awakening national consciousness, enhancing national physical education, instilling scientific knowledge, increasing productive power, stimulating inherent morality, rewarding diligence and thrift habits, cultivating a positive and upward outlook, and encouraging the spirit of sacrifice and struggle, all of which have been considered and implemented in stages, areas, and items to supervise and improve them. The educational cause of the province, in terms of quality, has already made significant progress. It is reported that in order to implement the established policy, the department has formulated 148 administrative plans for the entire year of the 25th year, which will be submitted for approval and then formulate an agenda for implementation in stages. It is also reported that according to the needs and possibilities of various actual situations in education and economics in the province, higher education will continue the policy of the previous year, responding to the need to cultivate talents. In secondary education, in addition to dedicating efforts to teacher training as the basis for qualitative improvement, special attention will be paid to the training of youth corps at all levels in order to enhance the effectiveness of education. In primary education, in addition to promoting compulsory education as much as possible and ensuring that the classes of existing primary schools at all levels are filled, the counties will be urged to hold short-term teacher training in stages to meet urgent needs and increase efficiency. In social education, the focus will be shifted to organizing and training the people, providing them with spiritual and special skills training so that they can become useful citizens of the modern state. Regarding local education funding, efforts will continue to be made to promote the movement to increase education funding and reorganize the educational funds and properties of various counties and cities as the first priority. Encouragement and reward will be used to supplement the inadequacies of administrative orders and supervision, and active guidance, assessment, and correction will be carried out in parallel to gather public and private talents and seek the rapid advancement of education in the province.

Shen Bao Medical and Pharmaceutical Supplement

Overview of the Treatment of Tonsil Diseases in Children in the Provincial Capital of Jiangsu 200

— Li Lingdong

—One of the Works of the Health Education Committee of the Provincial Capital of Jiangsu—

The importance of school health today has become an unbreakable fact in the current health and education sectors. Because school life is a stage that everyone must go through, lasting from a few years to two or three decades, almost all of humanity's wisdom and skills are cultivated in schools. However, we only pay attention to the academic instruction of children and neglect their physical health, the development of good hygiene habits, and as a result, children are physically weak, mentally and physically incomplete, prone to illness and lingering disasters, and the efficiency of teaching is weakened and reduced invisibly. Therefore, the promotion of school health really needs urgent development. For example, physical examinations, correction of defects, diagnosis, treatment and prevention of diseases, health education, and environmental health facilities, these are all the work of school health.

Correcting defects is one of the most important tasks of school health. All the physical health defects found during health examinations must be properly corrected to restore them to a normal state. Among the defect items, trachoma, tooth decay, and tonsils are the most common. The treatment of trachoma, ear diseases, and dental diseases can still be carried out in schools, but it is difficult to treat tonsils. Because the method of treating tonsils requires surgery, which takes time and requires a well-equipped hospital to perform. However, when the medical knowledge of the general parents of children is lacking, they do not know the harm of enlarged tonsils, and when they hear about the removal, they immediately refuse. Therefore, the treatment of tonsils is only seen in Nanjing, Shanghai, Beiping and other places, and the number of those who are treated is very few. From this, we can see that the treatment of tonsils is a major difficulty in the implementation of school health.

The Health Education Committee of the Provincial Capital of Jiangsu was established just two months ago. According to the results of health examinations of 2,800 students in seven primary schools in the provincial capital, about 20.71% of the students examined had enlarged tonsils. If these defects are not corrected, it will not be a way to protect the health of children in the long run. In December 24th year, the council decided to use the winter vacation period to carry out tonsil correction work. Later, with the assistance of Zhenjiang Christian Hospital, it agreed to allocate a special ward and provide various preferential measures, and the tonsil removal of this council was finally realized.

1. Outline of the Scheduled Methods for Tonsil Correction

2. Public Lectures: Using the time of the weekly memorial week of each school, this council will send doctors, health instructors and nurses to each school to give lectures on the harm of tonsils and their correction methods, so that students can understand and are happy to remove them.

3. Issuing Brochures: This council will compile a brochure explaining enlarged tonsils and distribute them to each school. All students with enlarged tonsils will receive one each, and the principal will order the students to bring them to their parents to read, so that the parents can understand and sympathize with the implementation of the removal period and are happy to assist.

4. Classroom Lectures: Using tonsils as a major unit center of teaching materials, so that students have a deep understanding of tonsils.

5. Arranging Students: Each school will compile a list of the names of students with enlarged tonsils, and then the doctors of this council will re-examine them. All students with enlarged tonsils who should be corrected immediately will have their addresses identified and listed in a table, so that they can start to persuade them to have the tonsils removed.

6. Parent-Teacher Conferences: Each school will convene the parents of students with tonsils, and the chief physician and nurses of this council will have individual talks with the parents to explain the harm of enlarged tonsils and simple correction methods, so that each parent can have a deep understanding of them and is willing to have their children receive tonsil correction.

7. Home Visits: Nurses will be assigned to visit each student's home in person, and will earnestly persuade and explain them. After obtaining the consent of the parents, they will be asked to sign and seal, and at the same time, they will give detailed instructions to each parent on the registration, examination, hospitalization, and payment procedures for guiding students to enter the Christian Hospital at the time.

8. Contact the Hospital: This council will negotiate with Zhenjiang Christian Hospital on all matters related to registration, outpatient, hospitalization, and payment preferential measures, and set detailed items for implementation. (To be continued)

Difficulties in Handling Rural Sanitation and Solutions (2) 201

— Liu Fangnong

(7) People Live Scattered: In the countryside, large villages have only a hundred or so households, small ones only ten or so, or even single-household villages, with each village at least a li or so apart. Sometimes, although there are many villages, the population is not large. According to past experience, in a place with six thousand people, even after two or three years of promotion, farmers still do not recognize the importance of medicine and hygiene.

(8) Staff Do Not Understand Farmers' Psychology and Rural Conditions: Many doctors and nurses, when they first come to serve in rural areas, do not know the rural organization and the psychology of the people, and do not understand in detail what rural sanitation is. They think that the experience of the hospital is hygiene, and they do not know what method to use to promote the sanitation cause. They do not know that treatment is only the starting point for prevention, so they do not have interest and effectiveness in their work.

(9) There are Many Quack Doctors in Rural Areas: These doctors often persuade people to have all-inclusive treatment. The medicines they use are mostly overbearing medicines such as promoting and reducing drugs, which can temporarily alleviate the symptoms or use symptomatic treatment to muddle through. When the disease recurs or worsens, they have already received the money and are not responsible for anything, escaping without a trace. Therefore, farmers are poisoned by them, thinking that only all-inclusive doctors can wholeheartedly diagnose and treat, and use good medicine. These are all common misconceptions. A doctor should have a compassionate heart, so how could they not carefully diagnose and treat? Moreover, new doctors never have all-inclusive treatment, and all-inclusive treatment is prohibited by law. In addition, farmers are often stubborn, and we have repeatedly seen them entangled with quack doctors because of all-inclusive treatment, which is a major obstacle to the future.

(10) Treatment Difficulties: Handling rural sanitation starts with treatment, but because the general farmers' knowledge is simple, they can be said to know nothing about medical knowledge. Therefore, those who come for treatment will ask what the disease is, how it will be tomorrow, how it will be the day after tomorrow, and how many days it will take to recover. Even the most experienced doctor cannot answer this kind of question immediately, right? Moreover, the diagnosis of many diseases cannot be known in a day or two. If you say how it will be tomorrow and how it will be the day after tomorrow, and it does not match tomorrow, then you will be questioned again. And if you often do not give him an answer, then he will often be suspicious. If one or two doses of medicine do not have a significant effect, then he will ask another expert. Quack doctors take the opportunity to fill their pockets again and again. When the disease enters a dangerous period, it often becomes incurable, which is a common fact that we see and hear.

(11) General Farmers are Obsessed with the Omnipotence of Medicine, Neglecting the Most Important Natural Therapy. For example, tuberculosis, in the current era, there is no specific medicine for treatment. The medicine known now cannot cure tuberculosis. The most important thing is to be quiet, rest, get plenty of fresh air and sunlight. If you tell them this kind of health preservation method, if they can accept it, they will be disheartened because they cannot get significant results in a short period of time, or because of work, they cannot continue to implement it in time. Therefore, they cannot understand the value of natural therapy, and think that relying on quiet rest cannot cure the disease. They often lightly let go of the cure period, relying solely on the omnipotence of medicine, requesting to take medicine, in vain turning the stomach into a natural medicine store. If this kind of dream is not broken, forgetting natural therapy, and only relying on taking medicine to cure lung disease, this is a great mistake. Not only is tuberculosis the case, but in fact, there are many diseases that also need to pay attention to natural therapy. Medicine is only the last resort of self-healing.

(12) Others, such as "New doctors (scientific doctors) are good at surgery, and Chinese doctors are good at internal medicine." This kind of absurd language has long been deeply imprinted in the minds of farmers. This is also a mistake in the concept of farmers.

The above twelve points are the facts experienced by the author. The following will briefly describe some remedial measures for the reference of comrades who are engaged in rural sanitation.

(1) Universal Education: "Universal Education" has been the most advocated argument since the September 18th Incident. Although in recent years, there have been facilities such as public schools and literacy compulsory classes in cities, the number of illiterate people in rural areas is shockingly high. However, the education expenses of farmers' land tax have been paid. Not only is there no way to enter higher education and secondary education, but there is also no opportunity to enjoy elementary education. If the people's knowledge is not open, the sanitation cause is naturally not easy to promote. Even the current strict prohibition policy is also because the people's knowledge is too shallow, "stubbornly ignoring government orders" and "regarding them as mere formalities" are also common occurrences. A few days ago, the Ministry of Education issued an order to set up rural schools everywhere. After we heard about it, we were overjoyed and wished that the authorities could realize it as soon as possible. Universal education is a sign of our national rejuvenation and national strength!

Since the anti-Japanese salvation movement in North China, there has been so-called "national disaster education". At this time when the national education textbooks are being reorganized, I hope that our education leaders can list hygiene as a basic subject. Because hygiene education is an important education related to the survival of the nation, we can adopt simple and easy-to-understand words as much as possible to instill knowledge about the causes of diseases, the prevention of diseases, personal hygiene, public hygiene, the benefits of new medicine, first aid methods, and the unreliability of asking gods and divination to students, so that they can plant the basic knowledge of simple medicine and hygiene when they are young. When the rural sanitation cause is developed and the rural sanitation personnel come to guide, they will easily accept it. Work such as home visits, infant care movements, maternal and child examinations, surveys of birth and death rates, and environmental sanitation will no longer be rejected or insulted. Moreover, they can also help where their abilities are lacking.

(2) Economic Source: Operating a business, of course, the presence or absence of money is the prerequisite condition. With money, everything can be done. This is undoubtedly a certain truth. However, there are good and evil in doing things. Like rural sanitation, it is a good thing that benefits society. However, in the minds of farmers in our country today, sanitation is not necessarily needed. If we want people to believe in sanitation, we must rely on the above-mentioned education and publicity, so that they can turn their painstaking efforts in believing in gods and divination to believing in our practically beneficial sanitation. Since they have the determination to believe, of course, for the sake of their own interests, they will also generate the power to generously donate and give assistance. However, relying solely on the fundraising of local people is not sustainable and is limited. It must rely on the government's regular expenses. If there is an insufficient amount, then the assistance of charitable organizations is required. Then the economic source is determined, and the person responsible for handling sanitation can rest assured to abide by their duties. At the same time, it can also increase the spirit of doing things. The equipment should be increased as appropriate, so as not to interrupt this great rural sanitation cause.

Common Knowledge Q&A About Diseases 202

— Cheng Hanzhang

(89) Kidney Stones (Part 1)

(Q) How are kidney stones formed?

(A) Our urine originally contains many crystalline substances that are dissolved in it and excreted from the body. If there is an obstacle and precipitation occurs, it can turn into sand and gravel in a certain part of the kidney. When it forms small particles, it is called kidney sand; slightly larger ones are called kidney gravel; larger ones are called kidney stones.

(Q) Is the formation of kidney stones in both sides at the same time?

(A) Usually, it is formed in the kidney pelvis on one side. If it goes down into the ureter, it becomes a ureteral stone; if it goes down further into the bladder, it becomes a bladder stone.

(Q) How many chemical components can be broken down when chemically analyzing this kind of kidney stone? What are the properties?

(A) The chemical components of kidney stones include urate, phosphate, and oxalate. Urate stones are brown or yellow, hard, with a smooth surface and layered cross-section. Phosphate stones are grayish-white and soft, can be crushed with two fingers, and are soluble in acetic acid. Most of them become bladder stones. Oxalate stones are made of calcium oxalate, dark brown in color, very hard, with a rough surface like mulberry, and a cross-section with money patterns, and are soluble in inorganic acids. In addition, there are carbonate stones. Cystiu stones, Xantlhin stones, ndigo stones, etc. are rare.

(Q) Under what circumstances does the body develop kidney stones?

(A) Before the formation of stones, there must be a matrix present, and urine must be abnormal at the same time. The matrix is ​​nothing more than epithelial fragments, mucus or blood clots, bacterial clumps, parasite eggs, etc.; then the stone components attach to it and become larger and larger. The reason why stone components precipitate from urine is the abnormality of urine concentration and reaction.

(Q) Are kidney stones related to the body or age?

(A) It is related to the inheritance of body constitution. Most of them are men aged 30 to 60. Children also develop them.

(Q) Is it related to life, diet, etc.?

(A) People who eat too much meat, drink alcohol, and often drink beverages with too much lime are prone to this disease.

(Q) Is the occurrence of kidney stones related to geography?

(A) There are more Westerners, especially in countries such as England, Russia, the Netherlands, and Germany. This is probably because their daily diet contains more salt.

(Q) What symptoms do patients present at the beginning of kidney stones?

(A) If the stones do not remain in the renal pelvis or calyx, or are very small and easy to excrete, they usually do not cause any symptoms. Sometimes pyelonephritis is triggered due to bacterial infection.

(Q) What symptoms do patients present when the stones gradually grow larger?

(A) Medium-sized mobile kidney stones are often embedded in the outlet of the renal pelvis or the ureter, thus causing a severe colic, called renal colic. A sharp pain in the kidney area occurs after body movements or suddenly. This severe pain goes down along the ureter, affecting the bladder or the inner side of the thigh or the back. The pain is sometimes strong and sometimes weak, and there are also points of tenderness. (To be continued)

Common Sense of Hygiene for Ear, Nose, Throat, and Eye Diseases 203

— Tang Renjin

(92) Talking About Changes in the Fundus From Nephritis (Part 2)

The symptoms of nephritis are very complicated. The main ones are proteinuria in which protein is mixed in the urine, hematuria in which blood is mixed, and the most dangerous uremia. However, there is a kind of physiological proteinuria that must be distinguished from it. That is, healthy people often find physiological proteinuria after walking for a long time, physical exertion, mental excitement, cold baths, and ingesting chicken eggs. This is what we must pay attention to. Hematuria is because the urine is mixed with a large amount of hemoglobin, so the urine often has a significant blood-like color. Hematuria can be divided into two types. One is hemoglobinuria. Red blood cells are mostly broken down, and free hemoglobin exists in the urine. One is hematuria. Red blood cells can generally maintain their original shape and are mixed in the urine. The symptoms of uremia can be divided into two types: neurological and inflammatory symptoms. In neurological symptoms, headache is often the most obvious. Headaches can often spread throughout the head, sometimes limited to the frontal, parietal, or occipital region. As for inflammatory symptoms, they are skin diseases, called uremic rash. The most common is chronic eczema. Uremia can sometimes also cause stubborn diarrhea, hoarseness, acute laryngeal edema, pneumonia, uremic pleurisy, myocarditis, peritonitis, pleurisy, uremic epistaxis, and uremic purpura, etc. dangerous diseases. If uremic spasm occurs in uremia, it is mostly fatal. Therefore, once a nephritis patient falls into uremia, it can indicate that it has reached a dangerous period. In addition, nephritis patients have a strong pale color of the skin (this is because the amount of red blood cells and hemoglobin decreases after the onset of the disease.) and skin edema. Edema initially occurs on the face, with obvious swelling of the eyelids. Therefore, the eyelid fissure is also narrowed. Soon, the skin of the whole body also develops strong edema.

After reading the above section, we can probably get a considerable understanding of nephritis. However, changes in the fundus are also important and should not be ignored. Because changes in the fundus can often be used as an aid to diagnosis. Therefore, doctors should first examine the urine when they suspect nephritis. At the same time, they should also examine the fundus, nothing more than to seek accurate diagnosis. However, this is not only the case with nephritis. Changes in the fundus are also often caused in diabetes, syphilis, tuberculosis, trauma, and arteriosclerosis. Therefore, it should also be checked in these situations. Changes in the fundus mostly belong to retinal diseases. Now, let me briefly describe retinitis caused by nephritis.

Nephritic retinitis, also known as albuminuric retinitis. Ten percent of nephritis patients can develop this disease. It is especially common when chronic nephritis transitions to renal atrophy, or during the progression of renal atrophy. It is also often found in gestational nephritis. Its symptoms are bleeding, white spots, and venous congestion and tortuosity in the retina of both eyes. The optic disc is also red, turbid, and swollen. Stellate white spots or large and small yellow spots occur in the periphery of the macular area and the vicinity of the optic disc. The patient feels that his vision is impaired. The prognosis of this disease is generally poor. Its treatment should focus on treating nephritis. Zhou Mengbai

Domestic Medicinal Plants (Continued) 204

— Zhou Mengbai

4. Wolfberry Lycium Chinense Mill

(Plant) It grows naturally in the wilderness, by the roadside, and is a deciduous small shrub. The small branches have thorns and often change. The leaves are soft, with petioles, lanceolate or obovate, with sharp or rounded ends. In summer, light purple bell-shaped flowers bloom from the leaf axils, and the petals are shallowly divided into five. The berries are elliptical, and turn red when ripe.

(Crude Drug) Cortex radicis Lycii (Wolfberry Bark), is the dried bark of its roots. This product is tubular or semi-tubular, 5 cm long and 1 cm thick. The surface is dirty yellow or yellowish-brown, the inner surface is light brown, the texture is rough and loose. The fracture surface is uneven. This product has a mild fragrance, and the taste is sweet first and then bitter, both slightly.

Folium Lycii (Wolfberry Leaves) are collected and dried leaves.

Fructus Lycii (Wolfberry Fruits) are collected fruits.

(Ingredients) Only Betaine has been proven to exist in the fruit.

(Medicinal Use) Old sayings: Wolfberry bark and wolfberry leaves have antipyretic effects. The wolfberry wine made from wolfberry fruit can be used as a tonic for the weak. Wolfberry wine is made by crushing five liters of wolfberry fruit (fresh), putting it in a silk bag, and then sealing it with two斗 of wine for cold soaking. It will be ready in two weeks.

Wolfberry wine nourishes deficiency, removes fatigue and heat, grows muscle, benefits complexion, and makes people fat and healthy. Wolfberry leaves are made into soup, slightly bitter. As the saying goes: "When leaving home for thousands of miles, do not eat Luomo wolfberry." This means that the two things supplement essence and qi, and strengthen the vagina.

Prescription Example: Ginseng Wolfberry Bark Powder, used to treat heat-clearing medicine for various symptoms of tuberculosis. Ginseng, Wolfberry bark, Bupleurum, Huangyin, Rehmannia Glutinosa, 15.0 each

Anemarrhena, Gypsum 15.0 each, Poria 7.5

The above is made into a decoction of 200, taken warm three times a day.

Q&A on Dental Knowledge (39) 205

— Lin Jianxian

(Question 304) Why do you sometimes need to use two kinds of materials to fill a deep cavity when the dental pulp is not dead?

Answer: Deep cavities are close to the dental pulp, so a layer of cement that is impervious to cold and heat should be laid first as a base, and then filled with metal.

(Question 305) What material is used to fill the root canal?

Answer: Fine strips made of rubber (commonly called artificial nerves) and a paste made of disinfectant are filled into the root canal. After the root canal is filled, a layer of cement is laid on it, and the remaining part can be completely filled with ordinary filling material.

Section 8 Extraction Problems

(Question 206) Which teeth should be extracted?

Answer: The following types should be extracted: (1) Cavities that cannot be filled and cannot be fitted with inlays; (2) Diseased teeth that cause severe pain and cannot be cured; (3) Teeth that have been loosened and cannot be firmly planted, or teeth that have been broken; (4) Diseased teeth that have become suppurated and are ineffective and endanger health; (5) Tooth roots that hinder the fitting of full dentures; (6) Useless and obstructive teeth, such as supernumerary ectopic teeth, etc.

(Question 207) What things should you tell the dentist before extraction?

Answer: Anyone with heart disease, people who are prone to bleeding, people who have nervous disorders or are prone to epilepsy, or people who have neurasthenia and have been insomnia for several days should tell the doctor about his suffering. If it is not suitable for extraction, you can stop or wait until the future to extract. Also, pregnant women who are four or five months pregnant should also tell the doctor. All these are for the sake of caution, so as to avoid the doctor from acting rashly without paying attention.

(Question 208) What time of day is the most suitable for extraction?

Answer: Morning is the most appropriate, and evening is not very appropriate.

(Question 209) Is tooth extraction painful?

Answer: In the past, tooth extraction was indeed a painful and terrible thing. But since the invention of very safe and effective anesthetics, unless there are special circumstances, it can be said that there is no pain at all, just like cutting hair and trimming nails, it is not a big deal.

(Question 210) Why should the patient be absolutely calm during the extraction?

Answer: Since tooth extraction is not painful and is performed in a formal dentist's office, and there is no danger, it is a very common thing and there is no reason to be afraid. If you are afraid, many difficulties will arise. Some occasional complications during tooth extraction are caused by the patient's panic, so the patient should be absolutely calm and have the kind of attitude described in the story of Guan Yu scraping bone to cure the disease and playing chess calmly. In ancient times, there was no anesthetic. If you are still afraid of tooth extraction safely and painlessly today, it is really a self-inflicted trouble and too unmanly.

After Old Cotton Stops New Trading; New Situation in the Yarn Market; Bulls and Bears Are Quite Willing to Settle at a Premium; The Exchange Is Holding a Meeting to Discuss Solutions 217

Recently, the yarn and cloth exchange market, because of the frequent accidents in the July and August old cotton futures, has been turbulent, with drastic ups and downs, as recorded in this newspaper. At the time of the routine settlement at the end of this month, there were huge storms on the two days before and after, and the competition between the bulls and bears was extremely fierce, which was rare in history. On the day before the delivery date (24th), the general speculators found great panic, and the market price rose in a straight line, like a tide, unstoppable, rising above the exchange's limit price, so both sides announced a suspension of trading, the highest point being 52.5 yuan, the sharpness of the rise was terrifying. It is said that although there are 100,000 dan of cotton that have passed the inspection at the inspection office, it is still short of the top cover, so there is a crazy rise. Unexpectedly (25th) was the last scene of the bulls and bears struggling. The first two sessions opened with a sudden sharp drop, with July falling by 3.5 yuan and August falling by 3 yuan, both exceeding the exchange's statutory suspension limit, and trading was also suspended. When trading opened in the afternoon, the bulls and bears were at odds, and the market was chaotic, with different opinions. Some said that the bulls were dissatisfied with the exchange's suspension of new trading and tried to settle as much as possible, causing the price to fall to the limit. Another said that a certain aspect had been compromised and a peaceful solution was announced. However, after a long period of chaos, the exchange was forced to the statutory limit price and was unable to open trading. As a result, the July and August futures were not traded at all. At this final stage of this month, such a huge storm was staged, causing the bulls and bears to be unable to make a full settlement, which is still a novelty. However, the general speculators were unable to receive the goods and were very eager to sell, shouting a price of 45.6 yuan, willing to get out. The exchange did not allow trading to open, and there was no result. After the market closed, the bulls and bears looked for accounts to settle at a premium, with the selling party settling at 1 yuan or 2 yuan lower than the listed price of 49 yuan. As a result, the remaining 121,200 dan, of which 20,000 were in stock, and 30,800 were in disaster relief, with a net stock of 90,400 dan. According to the market, the bulls will of course not follow the routine receiving rules because trading failed to open in the afternoon on that day. Another said that they had reached a compromise with the other party, and if the quality of the goods received was found to be substandard, etc., the exchange would be responsible for compensating for the price loss. There are conflicting rumors in the market, and no one knows the truth. The latest news is that the exchange is still holding a meeting to discuss solutions.

Piece Goods: Autumn Goods Are Selling Well; The Market is Gradually Rising 219

Cotton Cloth: Recently, because of the general positive sentiment in all areas regarding autumn dyeing and printed goods, such as printed flannel, colored striped flannel, white flannel, blue cloth, yuan twill, printed satin, Zhigong, serge, plain serge, Zhigong, thread tweed, large quantities of August and September futures have been ordered, the price is gradually rising, and the ordering parties continue to make orders, and the momentum is not weakening. All factories have thrown out huge amounts of futures, the price of printed flannel has increased from 1 jiao 6 fen to 1 jiao 8 and a half fen, and the price of serge has increased from 2 jiao 3 fen to 2 jiao 5 fen 75, and the prices of other goods have also increased uniformly, so the factories are eager to pull in gray cloth, and the annual regulations of Japanese factories stipulate that during this hot summer, before the new cotton comes on the market, the number of working days will be reduced by two days per week for one or two months, and the output will of course be greatly reduced. At the same time, the output of Chinese factories is also not enough to meet market demand. In previous years, this was the busy farming season, and the summer goods were declining, and the autumn goods were still lacking demand, and the factories were holding back goods, but this year there is this abnormal phenomenon, which is actually due to the currency problem and the abundant harvests in various places. Yesterday's market situation was still stable, the sales of white goods were flat, and only the four gentlemen serge and Zhigong of colored goods were still high in demand by Japanese merchants, and last Friday and Saturday they received scattered goods from the market, and the market rose sharply, soaring 7 and a half li per yard from the last market.

Woolen Cloth: The Shanghai offices of Sichuan and Guizhou merchants have recently received letters and telegrams, planning to buy woolen cloth, wide and narrow camel hair, plain serge, tweed, Walter tweed, yuan woolen felt, Melton, etc., which are needed for autumn sales, and transactions continue, and the market situation is quite good. Grain: Bulls Have No Intention of Continuing to Support; Wheat Flour Falls Sharply 220

Flour Exchange to Stop Afternoon Trading Starting Today 221

After the flour market opened in the morning, the market for each month was uniformly tired and sluggish. In the afternoon, the collapse was quite large. Initially, at 4 o'clock, there was a difference of about 1 jiao in the price of foreign wheat, and the market sentiment was that this month had already been settled according to the limit, and it was inferred from this that the market could no longer rise. Also, this year's summer harvest was reported to be abundant, and the main food was cheap, so the price of flour would naturally fall, so people's minds softened, and many bulls unloaded their goods, and the market was depressed. When trading opened in the afternoon, most of the bulls had no intention of continuing to support, and the flower and yarn market also reversed from high to fall, and people were inevitably worried, so the shouting price was greatly relaxed, and the fall was very large. After this situation, if the sales of flour are flat, it may still be soft.

Also, the Flour Exchange originally scheduled to close in the afternoon yesterday, but it was heard that the procedures had not yet been completed, so it was changed to close in the afternoon starting from July 28th. The morning session will start at 10 o'clock and trade in four sessions.

After the wheat market opened in the morning, the market for each month was generally flat and soft. Because the new rice harvest in the Yangtze River area this year was very abundant, people's minds in the industry had long been softened. As for the outside bulls, they were worried about the repetition of the flower and yarn market, so they seemed not to encourage it anymore, so the market was able to gradually move towards the right path and the shouting price was gradually loosened. When trading opened in the afternoon, the current month was the last day, and many of the industry's goods were withdrawn by themselves, so the market was still stable. As for August and below, because the flour market was falling sharply, most of the insiders and outsiders unloading high-priced goods were still able to stand firm, so the near term fell by 78 fen, and the far term fell by 1 jiao. The middle and lower grades are being suppressed by each factory everywhere, and the counter-offer is 1 jiao less than the previous week, so there is no transaction.

Statistics: Shanghai Living Expense Index 234

How Legal Tender and Smuggling Affect It

The Shanghai Municipal Social Bureau recently conducted a detailed study on the impact of the implementation of legal tender last November and the rampant smuggling that began this April on the city's living expense index. This is indeed a question worthy of attention. The Bureau has conducted a detailed study, and the main points are listed below:

Rent Category: In the past eight months, among all categories of indices, only the rent category has shown a downward trend. The rent index for 1936 was 116.78, which is 3.13% lower than the previous year. In the past three or four years, due to the economic downturn in the city, more and more houses have been left vacant. Initially, this did not affect workers' housing. However, since last year, due to factory closures and layoffs, workers' incomes have plummeted after unemployment or reduced working hours. As a result, they have taken their families back to their hometowns, or squeezed into their already cramped housing to reduce rent expenses. Therefore, rental advertisements were posted all over the workers' residential areas, both in the front and back buildings. Landlords reduced rents to rent out the houses as soon as possible to reduce the burden of vacant rooms. Some even considered it a daunting task due to the lack of profit. Entire buildings were also closed down. As a result, large landlords also followed suit and reduced rents. However, even with the rent reduction, workers still found it unbearable. Therefore, the current reduction in rent not only does not help improve workers' housing problems but also further reflects the economic recession in workers' lives.

Food Category: The implementation of legal tender did not have much impact on rice prices. The food category index for November 1935 was 90.63, which is only 2.42% higher than the previous month. In December, the index continued to decline due to the downward trend in rice prices. Although rice prices fell further in January of this year, other items such as flour, vegetables, and soybean oil all became more expensive. The index for this category rose to 95.93. In March, it continued to increase to 99.89. In April, the price of Xian rice suddenly increased, but vegetable prices generally fell, and the index fell to 94.51. However, in May and June, rice prices continued to fall, and the index fell further to 93.48 and 93.69.

Clothing Category: The clothing category index for November last year was 86.14, which is 4.31% higher than the previous month. This is because the prices of various items rose with the implementation of legal tender. The index continued to rise in December and January. The index for January was 90.88. In February, it rose further to 93.01. In March and April, the prices of fine cloth, striped cloth, and woolen cloth fell, and the index hovered around 91.50. From May onwards, due to the impact of smuggling, the prices of goods plummeted, and the index fell to around 87.

Fuel Category: The index for this category in October 1935 was 125.10. In November, it rose sharply to 142.93, which is 14.25% higher than the previous month. This was due to the sudden increase in kerosene prices. The index continued to rise to 150.25 in January of this year. In February, March, and April, it slightly returned to 146. From May onwards, affected by kerosene smuggling, it fell to 142.54. In June, it fell further to 138.62.

Miscellaneous Category: In October last year, the index for this category was 116.96. In November, it suddenly rose to 128.20, which is 9.6% higher than the previous month. Before the currency reform, the exchange rate of copper coins fluctuated constantly. Most miscellaneous items were purchased with copper coins, so the index's ups and downs were often affected by changes in the exchange rate of copper coins. In October last year, one yuan could be exchanged for 337 coins. On November 4, it suddenly shrank to 299 coins. Soon after, the Ministry of Finance stipulated that each yuan should be worth 300 copper coins and should not fluctuate. As a result, the exchange rate stabilized, and the index for this category also remained around 125.00 with very little change.

General Living Expenses (Total): In October 1935, it was approximately 97.54. In November, due to currency changes, the index rose to 101.49, which is 4.05% higher. In other words, the purchasing power of silver dollars in October was 102.52, while in November, it was only 98.3. In November, it slightly rebounded, and from January of this year, it gradually increased. In March, the index reached 107.10, which is 9.80% higher than in October last year. From April onwards, due to the impact of smuggling, commodity prices fell, and the index gradually declined. By June, it was only 102.74, but it was still higher than before the implementation of legal tender. (The rest is omitted)

Chun Qiu (Spring and Autumn)

Tidbits 235

— (Lu Changfan)

Modern people take life too lightly. Just look at the Shanghai Municipal Social Bureau's statistics on suicides: on average, one person commits suicide every four hours." No! Some people take life too seriously. Just listen to the phrase "A beggar's life." From the above two points, life can be divided into two categories: Life, as light as a feather: Life, heavier than Mount Tai.

"Which is cleaner, 'death' or 'life'?" If you ask the majority of the people this question, you will know if their answers are correct or not. I dare to say one thing, they always answer like this: "Of course death is cleaner!" We need to study why they answer this way. The question is easy to answer: they think that the filth they can see is filth. In fact, the filth that cannot be seen is much filthier than the filth that can be seen. It is like the great powers slaughtering our soldiers and civilians with guns and cannons and invading our land with force. In their eyes, that is slaughter and invasion. They are unaware of things like economic invasion…

Gleanings from the Women's Quarters 236

— Nanhai Seagull

When idly reading the poems and songs of the ancients, descriptions of the emotions of women in their quarters make up the largest part of the rhymes. Among them, descriptions of the indescribable places between the two sexes often make the reader feel as if they are in the scene, as if they are seeing the person, and their hearts are swaying uncontrollably. However, these are mostly written by thick-skinned male poets.

Women's shyness is heavier than men's. Although women's poetry and songs are rich in feminine beauty, they still dare not reveal very obscene and frivolous words. But there are also exceptions. For example, Ding Liuniang's "Ten Request Songs" in the Sui Dynasty are such lovely lyrics. Among them, one song about requesting a flower pillow says: "Under the green curtains in the orchid room, the mandarin duck brocade is spread on the lotus bed. It is appropriate to enjoy the happy feelings early, and the secret intentions must be shared. If you want to be intimate, ask Lang for a flower pillow."

Another example is Luo Aiai's quatrain "Giving to Lang": "Qilang's thousand gold intentions, holding Lang to sleep with delicate charm. Try making sounds in the curtain, shyly opening your eyes in front of the lamp." Such delicate and sensual words are truly written as if drunk and crazy.

Feng Ji of the Tang Dynasty has a poem "Divine Rooster Pillow": "The pillow painted with mandarin ducks has been resting for a long time, the new misty valley is cut to fight the divine rooster. Dreaming sweetly with Lang and forgetting the dawn, the rooster is also reluctant to crow."

Literary works are a reflection of personality. Women's chastity is mostly due to their nature. Li Jilan, a talented woman of the Tang Dynasty, wrote about roses when she was five or six years old: "Having not married for a long time, my thoughts are chaotic and horizontal." Her father was displeased when he saw it and said, "She will surely be a woman of lost conduct in the future." Later, she did become a courtesan with open social interactions between men and women. Once, she gathered with a group of worthies, and Liu Changqing had impotence. Ji Lan teased him with a set phrase: "Is the exhalation good day and night?" Liu blurted out, "The birds are happy to have a place to rest." Her sensuality was like this.

There was also Ms. Xue Tao, a famous courtesan of the Tang Dynasty. When she was more than ten years old, one day her father pointed to the Chinese parasol tree in the patio and sang, "A single ancient Chinese parasol tree in the courtyard, its trunk soars into the clouds." He ordered Tao to continue. Tao said: "Branches welcome birds from the north and south: leaves send off the wind from the past and the future." Her father was displeased for a long time. Later, Xue Tao entered and exited the town's tent, serving eleven towns, all of which were known for poetry. The people who came and went and sang with her included Yuan Zhen, Bai Juyi, Niu Sengru, Linghu Chu, Pei Du, Zhang Ji, Liu Yuxi and other famous scholars. In her later years, she lived in Huanhua, Sichuan, and built a poetry building. She lived to be seventy-two years old.

If Li Jilan and Xue Tao were born in this world, they would surely be strong generals in the women's movement, speaking out for the oppressed women.

A Discussion of an Insurance Transaction 237

— Pillow Green

A friend who works at a foreign insurance company told me the following story: A certain Westerner, a wealthy man and a fire insurance policyholder, one day brought a carpet to the company's manager. After a courteous greeting, he unfurled the carpet, which was quite luxurious, but with a hole burned in the side. He claimed that due to carelessness while smoking a cigarette, ash fell and the embers caused the damage. He sought compensation of one hundred dollars, the value of the new carpet, producing the original invoice as proof. The company manager examined it, saw the charred edges of the hole, and immediately approved the compensation as requested.

I commented, "The speed of the compensation is a common occurrence, but the reason behind the agreement between the client and the company is that everyone regards the small hole burned by a cigarette ash, which is insignificant, as being in accordance with the fire insurance contract, and they fulfill the terms without any doubt. This is commendable!"

Someone asked, "If this policyholder were Chinese, would he receive the same treatment?"

I would reply, "It's a pity this policyholder isn't Chinese; otherwise, the company could publicize its gratitude in the newspaper! Why wouldn't they happily use this incident as a means of attracting business with such a small expense?"

Someone else might say, "He is wealthy. He carelessly caused the damage himself, yet he seeks compensation for the full value. Isn't this being overly meticulous and showing a lack of generosity?"

I would reply, "Where reason lies, even the smallest amounts matter: this is close to being in accordance with the right path. Otherwise, how can the spirit of an industry be demonstrated and reach its full potential? The matter concerns mutual assistance, and the intention is beautiful. Business owners should strive to uphold this. Unfortunately, many Chinese merchants are focused on short-term gains and fail to understand this. The decline of many industries is partly due to this!"

Props! 238

— Nineteen

Ever since the Little Mermaid became a sensation both domestically and internationally, the average Miss is now willing to spend some of her time spent at dance halls and movie theaters by the swimming pool. Freestyle, breaststroke, backstroke: these new terms are now on their lips, as familiar as their own treasures.

Swimming, in the eyes of country folk, is a mundane affair. On hot summer days, even young children with yellowish hair will paddle in the ponds, splashing water for fun. They don't know any strokes, they don't wear swimsuits, they don't need any "sweethearts" to support them, and they don't want to show off. They only know how to enjoy themselves, completely different from the Misses in the city. The Misses' point of pride may lie in this very difference.

A friend told me that at a certain swimming pool, hordes of Misses flock there. Of course, in such a setting, there is a group of heroes who follow them, fulfilling the responsibility of supporting and protecting them; and the Misses also need these heroes to embolden them. Because of this, disputes over "props" have escalated beyond control, even developing into full-scale brawls.

What is a prop? This is quite interesting. It turns out that when these Misses are about to swim, they already have a sense of being on the edge of an abyss; especially at the moment of jumping in, their hearts beat proportionally with the splashing of the pool water. Therefore, there are heroes who are willing to lurk in the pool, to give them a "prop" at that last moment! It is said that this "prop" brings the heroes unexpected pleasure; and for the Misses, it can slightly reduce their fear. Who props whom, of course, each has their own territory. Mistaken props can be forgiven; but if someone tries to take over another's prop, or harbors inappropriate expectations, then the heroes will become enraged and become mortal enemies.

Mysterious, this "prop"!

Switched Destinies of Phoenixes 240

— Written by Zhang Henshui

Chapter 4: Doubts Rise and Fall with Sight and Sound, Letters Are Exchanged; Life and Death Can Be Entrusted, and Laments Are Sent with Generosity

Guoqi laughed: "Scholarly types are like that; they like to wage endless literary battles over a few words in an article. "Aunt Zhang nodded and smiled: "I understand that now; you must be fighting literary wars with people in the newspaper again." Even if it's such a thing, winning is winning, and losing is losing; it's not like you're losing sesame seeds or soybeans. Why be in such a hurry?" Guoqi laughed: "That's what you call a scholar's perspective. Since Mom doesn't approve of such things, I won't reply to the letter." Aunt Zhang looked at his face and saw that his smile was still natural, so she took out the glasses she had placed in her pocket and put them on her nose. She nodded and said, "When dealing with outsiders, you should always take the path of least resistance. Saving a bit of effort with outsiders means having more effort for your own matters. Don't you think so?" Guoqi stood in the hall, looking very relaxed, looking up at the sky, and then humming an English song under his breath. He glanced at his mother and saw that she had lowered her head and was doing needlework again. Only then did he walk back to his room, put the letters back in the suitcase, and then locked the suitcase. Aunt Zhang said, "It's time for class; you can go now, right?" Guoqi said, "Not in a hurry." As he said this, his face was gentle and happy. He picked up his satchel, adjusted the brim of his felt hat, and walked out the front door as if nothing had happened. But as soon as he left the house, the situation changed drastically. He slowly lowered the hand holding his books, and his head drooped, looking only at the few feet of road in front of him. If the road from his home to the school wasn't so familiar, he really wouldn't know where he was going. He walked into the school in a daze and went straight to the campus from the school gate. On the campus, two tall phoenix trees shaded a horizontal stone bench, which was partially blocked by a small rose trellis. This was a quiet and comfortable place. So he put his satchel on the stone bench and sat there, lost in thought. He sat for a long time, then took off his hat and continued to sit there in a daze. Finally, the sound of the bell rang, waking him up. He stood up, sighed, and said, "I'm being a bit silly; let it go." Then he picked up his hat and satchel and went to the classroom to teach. Because of an indescribable feeling in his heart, he didn't go to the library to read the newspaper, nor did he look for colleagues to talk to. He walked home without enthusiasm. Of course, he didn't deliberately take the road to wait for that person, as he had done in the past few days. He walked straight down the shortest road, without thinking about anything else. (53)

Personal Vignettes

The Life of Gorky (Part 1) 241

— Lin Liqin

Maxim Gorky, the only great writer of our time, is dead. This is the greatest misfortune for the literary world and an irreparable loss! We should express our final respect for his sudden passing, by draping a black veil in the garden of literature to mourn the fall of this brilliant star.

Today, we unanimously mourn Maxim Gorky, who is not only the mentor of Soviet proletarian literature, but whose noble position has already firmly occupied the throne of the authority in the world's literary scene. Gorky's enthusiastic commitment to the construction and creation of his country's new society, as well as his dedication to the working class and his efforts for the victory of Bolshevism in his brilliant writings; especially his admirable spirit of perseverance and tenacity during the era of Nicholas II's violence when he participated in revolutionary work. Therefore, Gorky's death should be mourned by all the people of the Soviet Union and their party and government leaders, and Gorky's death should be recognized as the second greatest loss to the Soviet Union after the death of Lenin.

Here, because of Gorky's greatness, I feel that writing a few ordinary words of mourning is too small and too meager. Therefore, I have changed to writing a few sketches about his life and a cross-section of his art here, to serve as a reverent eulogy for us to present to him—however, due to my shallow understanding, there will inevitably be many errors.

Gorky's name encompasses the Earth like air, but "Maxim Gorky" is just a pen name. His real name is Alexey Maximovich Peshkov. He was born on March 29, 1868, in Nizhny Novgorod in central Russia. In his childhood, he was born into a working-class family, and the family was too poor to afford to send him to school.

In 1878, when Gorky was ten years old, in the autumn of that year, he began to earn a living with his own strength and became an apprentice in a shoemaker's shop. The following year, he switched from the shoemaker's shop to work as an apprentice in a drafting office. But what he learned there was not drafting, but the work of a servant who did washing and sweeping.

In the spring of 1880, Gorky, whose living conditions were too painful, escaped from the drafting office to the banks of the Volga River, where he became an apprentice to a cook on a ship. The cook, named Smury, was a thoughtful and studious retired sergeant with a kind and gentle disposition. From him, Gorky began to understand the taste of reading.

In 1883, Gorky's increasing interest in reading made him realize that he should seek some systematic knowledge. So he wandered alone to Kazan, secretly hoping to enter Kazan University to study. However, this ideal was immediately shattered by reality after he tried it once; because the institutions of higher learning during the Tsarist era were set up exclusively for cultivating sons and daughters of wealthy families, how could they allow barefoot poor boys to cross the threshold! He had no choice but to reorganize his labor and enlist in a local bakery as a deputy. In Kazan, although his ambition to study had been dashed, he inadvertently gained the opportunity to get close to people in the intellectual class, and also joined the organization of reading clubs; thus he learned a little about the general situation and darkness of politics at that time, and inspired his future revolutionary thoughts; and also gained many experiences of inhuman life from personal experience, so as to create his future great creation. He lived in Kazan for four or five years, working hard in the factory, while also diligently reading works such as Dostoevsky's "Poor People". Later, his passion for the revolution increased, and he joined the group of so-called "people being watched", starting his actual revolutionary activities. Thus, Gorky's actions also began to be noticed by detectives.

In 1889, at the age of twenty-one, Gorky had returned to his hometown—Nizhny Novgorod from his wandering journey. This year, he was subjected to conscription inspection, and was exempted from military service because his lungs were not healthy. He worked as a clerk in a lawyer's office—the lawyer's name was Lanin, who had a great influence on Gorky's future: he read many books from this lawyer; and for this reason, in October of this year, he was arrested and imprisoned for the first time for reading special kinds of books that were not in accordance with his knowledge and education and that were not needed.

In 1891, at the age of twenty-three, Gorky left his hometown again and drifted to Tiflis, the capital of the Caucasus, where he worked in a railway factory. He used his spare time to write down his experiences and observations, and wrote his debut work "Makar Chudra". On September 25 of the following year, he signed the pen name "Maxim Gorky" and published it in the local newspaper "Caucasus" in Tiflis. From here, Gorky's literary career began—forty years later, on the same day of the same month in 1932, the Soviet people and party and government leaders held an unprecedented grand celebration to commemorate Gorky's forty years of literary life. The Soviet government awarded the most honorable Lenin Medal to Gorky in return for his revolutionary achievements, and the celebration decided to rename Nizhny Novgorod as "Gorkygrad" to commemorate Gorky's childhood life there.

Extra Supplement of the "Shen Bao" in this Locale

On Electric Therapy for Gonorrhea 242

— (Yaozu)

Electric therapy today is regarded in the medical community as the standard for treating all kinds of diseases, especially gonorrhea among venereal diseases. For example, Thias electric therapy is used for acute cases, and shortwave diathermy is used for chronic cases, both achieving good results. This is because gonorrhea germs, when exposed to electric heat above 42 degrees, will be eliminated without residue even if they are deeply hidden. The acute symptoms of gonorrhea are redness and swelling of the urethra's mucous membrane, pus dripping, severe pain and itching. Urinating makes it especially bad, often causing redness and swelling of the foreskin, inflammation of the inguinal lymph nodes, blood in the urine, and white clumps and strands clearly visible in the urine. In this acute stage, Thias electric therapy is the only treatment, and it is not difficult to cure when combined with injections and internal medicine. Chronic cases are transformed from prolonged acute gonorrhea. There is yellow mucus in the urine, mixed in the urethra. The opening of the urethra is sealed with pus in the morning. Sometimes there is a feeling of itching or burning, but swelling and pain are not severe. But if proper care is not taken at this time, the symptoms can worsen at any time. Epididymitis, cystitis, prostatitis, arthritis, etc. often occur at this time. Therefore, if gonorrhea has entered the chronic stage, shortwave diathermy and various appropriate treatments must be applied. The Father and Son Hospital in Shanghai offers fair prices and the most complete electrical therapy equipment for treating gonorrhea. With decades of experience, combined with the help of electrical therapy, it is no wonder that miraculous effects can be obtained.

A Record of Curing Ten Years of Ringworm 243

— (Manuscript by Yao Ruinian)

I have suffered from ringworm for almost ten years since I was in my twenties. It first appeared on both sides of my groin, then spread to my abdomen, and later to my neck, arms, and other places. For years, it has come and gone unpredictably, causing me much pain and itching. My skin was covered with sores, making me look dirty and unbearable. I have been struggling for food and clothing for years, and I already felt mentally and physically exhausted. This skin disease made me feel even more pain.
