Cantonese Settle Old Scores with Chen Jitang 255

— Me

According to a Hong Kong telegram from the previous day, Chen Jitang was ordered by the central government to remain in Guangdong until the province was handed over clearly. Another telegram stated that Chen Jitang moved into a foreign hospital on the 24th because Cantonese were pursuing old debts. Lin Yizhong suggested that if Chen was unable to obtain a passport to go abroad, he should first take refuge in Taiwan and then go elsewhere. All the gold, silver, and valuables, valued at more than 80 million yuan, were secretly stored in a certain foreign bank at the request of Chen Weizhou. More than 70 former employees of the Guangdong Headquarters and the Executive Committee came to Hong Kong from the province on the evening of the 24th to demand living expenses from Chen Jitang because their salaries had not been paid. Judging from the above two news items, Chen Jitang's departure this time did not clarify the handover procedures, and the salaries of his subordinates were not paid. This huge debt should be settled with Chen Jitang. Not only should the central government settle accounts with Chen Jitang, but the general officials and people of Guangdong Province should also settle accounts with Chen Jitang and must not let him off easily.

Chen Jitang stubbornly resisted the central government's orders in the Southwest for many years. However, he falsely claimed that Guangdong Province was experiencing economic difficulties and demanded subsidies from the central government. On the one hand, he closed the door and imposed heavy taxes, including opium taxes, gambling taxes, and various exorbitant taxes, layer by layer, draining the wealth of the people of Guangdong Province. Therefore, upon his resignation and departure, all his gold, silver, and property were valued at more than 80 million yuan. Where did this wealth come from? It was nothing more than the blood and sweat of the Cantonese people. Since Chen had so much property but refused to pay the salaries of his subordinates, he plundered the people's wealth for his own private gain. As for local construction projects, he often used the excuse of financial exhaustion and was unable to carry them out wholeheartedly. The four words "harming the country and the people" are truly appropriate for Chen. Now that he has left, if this debt is not settled with him, what other debts can be settled? If we don't settle with him now, when will we settle?

Chen Jitang dominated the Southwest and resisted the central government's orders for several years. The central government, aware of the inappropriateness of internal wars and the necessity of unification through orders, did not hesitate to compromise and seek solutions through peaceful means. However, Chen was cunning and fickle and had absolutely no sincerity. The domestic pacification efforts were difficult to achieve, and natural efforts to resist foreign aggression could not be started. As a result, the situation in the Northwest became unmanageable. Who should bear this responsibility? None other than Chen. Now that Chen has left, the people have suffered greatly from the situation that has been delayed for several years. Even if Chen had to resign and leave due to internal resistance, it would take even more effort to clean up this defeated situation. Therefore, Chen's departure this time should not only be accounted for economically but also for disrupting national unity.

Chen served as the King of the South for many years, causing the country to be divided. The central government was completely unable to effectively control the political, military, and economic policies. His crimes are too numerous to count. Now that he has left, he is taking more than 80 million yuan worth of gold, silver, and treasures to become a wealthy foreigner in a foreign country. This is too comfortable. To whom can the ordinary officials in Guangdong Province who are owed salaries and the suffering people turn to shed their tears? Therefore, I say that this bad debt of Chen Jitang's should not only be settled by the central government but also by the officials and people of Guangdong Province.

Swimming and Morality 256

— Fang Kewen

According to reports, while our government is sending male and female swimming athletes to the World Games, the authorities in North China have "ordered the city government to seal off" swimming pools because "mixed swimming by men and women is detrimental to morality."

A friend of mine saw this news and agreed, saying that swimming should be banned in China. He went on to explain his reasons, saying: In our so-called swimming pools, it's more like soaking in the water than swimming. Most of the women go to take photos so that they can be published in some pictorials with words like "swimmer" or "good swimmer." Most of the men have ulterior motives, using the pretext of swimming to get close to women. Even if someone goes to swim for real and becomes famous through swimming, they will only become a few more "mermaids" for a bunch of boring guys to idolize, like they are worshiping actors, acting as their handlers and biographers. Therefore, his conclusion is that swimming has a hundred harms and no benefits and should be banned.

My friend is quite "old-fashioned." He usually likes to quote some scriptures to explain that the "human heart is no longer ancient, and the world is getting worse." This time, of course, it is also "ancient," but I still write down his words here. This is not because I also like to be fashionable (China is an "ancient" country, and this year is a year of worshiping the "ancient"!) and learn to be "ancient." It is because many of the things he said are indeed true phenomena. If we do not shy away from seeking medical treatment for our illnesses, then these words need to be savored.

However, I cannot agree with his point of view, and therefore I do not agree with his proposition.

It is a fact that many young ladies go to swimming pools to take photos, and many young masters go to swimming pools with certain ulterior motives. However, what percentage does this account for? Looking at the new relationships between men and women with old eyes will always lead to the conclusion that they are "detrimental to morality." Isn't walking hand-in-hand on the road also "detrimental to morality" in the eyes of those who uphold morality? Moreover, can't "morality" be harmed by anything other than swimming? (Secretly marrying three or five wives, or even fewer, isn't that what moralists who claim to uphold "morality" often do? That is truly "detrimental to morality"!) Is it fair to take a part for the whole?

Furthermore, can we deny the meaning of swimming based on the "ugly deeds" of a few so-called "loose women and prostitutes"? Isn't banning swimming with things that have nothing to do with swimming itself an act of giving up eating for fear of choking? This is what wise people do.

As for the lesson of the "mermaid," it has nothing to do with swimming itself. Anyone who understands things a little knows this. The old society always regarded women as toys. Once an outstanding toy appeared, those in power would play with it in a joking manner because it was new. A group of flattering followers would immediately cheer and shout to create momentum in order to cater to the pleasure of those in power, and they would also make some money in the middle. As for those who were being praised, they would be flattered because their will was weak and their knowledge was insufficient.

Moreover, what is the current situation in North China? This is something that readers know as well as they know the palms of their hands. We really "don't want to say everything." In this dangerous environment where there is no room to breathe, they are still leisurely paying attention to swimming pools and "detrimental to morality." This makes us unable to think of any other reason besides guessing that it is "everyone for themselves," or diverting public attention. Could it really be that we are calling on people to use "morality" to resist the enemy's military, cultural, economic, and other aggressions?

A Visit to the Shanghai Frog Farm 257

— Fang Zhou

(Special Report) In recent years, many Chinese people have devoted themselves to productive industries, especially the promotion of rural sideline occupations, such as chicken farming, beekeeping, pigeon breeding, and rabbit raising. Nowadays, there are no shortage of people who are improving animal husbandry everywhere, and livestock farms have been established almost everywhere.

Our country has always been known in the world as an agricultural country. It has a vast land, abundant resources, a mild climate, and rich mountains, rivers, and land. The abundance of native products is enough to lead all countries in the world. Furthermore, statistics show that more than 70% of the people in the country are farmers. Unfortunately, the Chinese people stick to old methods and do not know how to improve, and the authorities in power have not paid attention to this. Therefore, the great resources are allowed to be buried, and rural bankruptcy has become the fatal injury to our country's economic downturn. However, when we look back at European and Western countries and Japan, can we not be awakened by their tireless research and promotion of productive industries?

However, in these two years, there have been many emerging industries discovered, such as goat milk farms and frog farms. I believe that as long as the government can protect and encourage these emerging industries, and the people can promote and improve them, then not only will their future development be limitless, but they will also greatly help the rural economy.

Frog farming is still an innovation in our country, and it is surprising to many people. However, it has long been very developed in Europe, America, and Japan. Moreover, the United States and Japan have established large-scale frog farms. In addition to frog meat for food, frogs can also be made into many leather goods. For example, the United States now has the manufacture of frog skin ties, frog skin shoes, frog skin briefcases, etc., but their prices are very expensive and not affordable for ordinary people.

Frogs are beneficial insects in the farm. They can prey on pests and protect crops. There is a folk saying in my hometown: "One frog watches over seven rice plants," which shows the contribution of frogs to protecting crops.

The Shanghai Frog Farm was founded by Mr. Shen Zhaoming and has only been around for a year. He initially purchased only six pairs of original rare giant frogs from a frog farm in Seattle, USA. Now, in addition to those that have been distributed, there are still more than ten pairs of frogs and tens of millions of small frogs and tadpoles on his farm.

Its address is on Memorial Road at the Jiangwan Sports Association. Yesterday, after taking a public bus to Jiangwan, it took me a long time to find a small sign on a fence that read "Shanghai Frog Farm, South from Here." So, I walked along the fence and saw a yellow wall with a big frog character on it across a field. Below it was a not-so-large fenced garden.

As I walked to the wooden fence gate, I was about to raise my hand to knock on the door when a dog suddenly rushed out from inside. Fortunately, the wooden fence gate was closed, or there would have been a risk of being bitten! Later, a person came out from inside and shooed the dog away. At the same time, he greeted me. I explained my intentions to him, and he expressed great pleasure and led me into the garden.

"Mr. Shen is still working in the office in Shanghai at the moment. He will be back at six o'clock, but he is here on Saturday afternoons and Sundays," he said to me as he walked.

This garden occupies more than three acres of land. The outer part is the frog farm's office and Mr. Shen's private residence. The inner part has a total of five large and small frog ponds, one is a frog breeding pond, one is a new frog pond, one is a tadpole pond, and another one raises Guangdong field chickens. One is empty and prepared for replacement. Each pond is separated by a board fence, and there is a lawn on the side of the pond for frogs to rest on the shore or prey on insects. The surface of the pond is covered with reed mats to avoid the hot sun.

The size of the frog pond is about fourteen or five square feet and two or three feet deep. However, the new frog pond seems to be larger, and the tadpole pond is the smallest. There are electric lights installed on the side of the pond to attract moths and other insects for the frogs to prey on. Frog breeding and management are easier than any other animal, and they do not need to be fed any kind of feed. They will grow and reproduce on their own.

It is said that each breeding frog can lay 10,000 eggs. After they are laid, they must be separated into different ponds, otherwise, when the tadpoles hatch and can crawl, they will be eaten by the mother frog. At least eight or nine new frogs can hatch from these 10,000 eggs. New frogs must be two years old before they can reproduce, and their reproductive capacity is very strong.

I will now briefly introduce the life of frogs and the benefits of frog farming for general rural sideline operators to use as a reference.

Frogs are amphibians with vertebrae. They have short and broad bodies, protruding eyes, and large mouths. Their front legs are short and their hind legs are long. When they are stretched out and lying flat, they look very much like a human. They are good at jumping and swimming, afraid of sunlight, and always like to come out at night to move. They often live in ponds and paddy fields, searching for grasshoppers, locusts, nymphs, mosquitoes, and all kinds of insects for food. They are very beneficial to crops.

The mating season is from March to April every year. In early summer, they lay their eggs in the water and grass in the pond, where the male frogs guard them. The eggs are in a kind of transparent and slippery liquid and gradually hatch into larvae - tadpoles. After three months, they become frog-shaped, and after five or six months, they can completely become frogs. As for the life of a frog, it is said to be eight or nine years long, but its reproductive capacity declines after five or six years.

Summer is the season when frogs are active, but every winter

Page 20

When winter arrives, the frogs hibernate in the soil, overwintering without eating or moving. There is no need to manage them at this time. They will come out again when the spring warms up. Therefore, winter is the resting period for frog farmers.

Frog farming is not only simpler and easier than any other animal husbandry, but it is also low-cost and high-profit. This is because frog farms do not require vast land or elaborate buildings. Two or three acres of land and a few hundred yuan of capital can start a frog farm, and one or two people are enough to manage the farm.

Frogs raised by oneself are fatter and more tender than ordinary ones, and each one weighs two or three pounds. Their taste is delicious and contains a large amount of nutrients. They are very rich in protein, and eating them is very beneficial to the human body. Therefore, I think that frog farming is a new and promising industry that is worth promoting, whether in cities or in the countryside, and I expect that its demand will be as widespread as fish and meat in the future.

After visiting the frog pond, I went to their office and sat for a while. In a glass bottle on the desk, a dead giant frog was soaked in alcohol. I looked at its shape and felt a little scared. According to the administrator, this giant frog was accidentally killed during customs inspection when it was shipped from the United States. Now, their farm has a limited number of frog breeds, and there are many people from all over the world who want to order them, such as Nanjing Jinling University and various livestock farms, agricultural schools, or private individuals. Therefore, there is a great shortage of supply. From this, we can see a glimpse of the attention that the Chinese people are paying to the frog farming industry.

The price of this frog breed is very high. Original rare giant frogs that are more than two years old (can reproduce in the current year) cost 24 yuan per pair, and new frogs that are less than one year old (can reproduce in two years) also cost 12 yuan per pair. There are even some that cost more than 30 or 40 yuan.

On the way back, I also asked them for a copy of "The Practical Frog Farming Method" compiled by Mr. Huang Zhongcheng.

— Liao Chuxiu

The lotus has the most names. Unopened ones are called "Hanyu," opened ones are called "Furong," and also "Fuyu." The fruit room is called "Lian," the leaves are "He," and the stem is "Ou." There are naturally other names, but I am too ignorant to know them.

The Song Dynasty Neo-Confucianist Zhou Mou used the lotus to compare to a "gentleman." His "Ode to the Lotus" was once selected for textbooks and is still praised by some people today. In fact, long before that old gentleman, during the time of Wu Zetian, who was deeply grieved by the Neo-Confucianists for "defiling the imperial harem," there was already a saying that the flower was used to compare to her lover, Zhang Changzong, the Sixth Prince. "The Sixth Prince is as beautiful as a lotus flower, but the lotus flower is not as beautiful as the Sixth Prince." Isn't this a famous story from ancient times to the present? The Furong in the "Song of Everlasting Regret," "face like a lotus flower, eyebrows like willow leaves," is also the lotus flower, not the Hibiscus mutabilis of melancholy wind and dew, and lonely autumn rivers. Suffering to the point that our bellies are empty, and we are about to lose our livelihoods. Livelihoods, forever poor, forever poor, wake up! Wake up! Everyone together, unite successfully, move forward, move forward! United as one! We hope that the government will raise a large amount of capital to manufacture trawlers. We hope that the government will not relax negotiations and do its best to make the big plan a success.

(4) Thirty million miles, which country has 3,000 miles of coastline? The Republic of China has 30 million miles of coastline, with 270,000 miles of large fishing area. Alas, our country's national power is too weak, and our territorial rights are being bullied. It is hateful that enemy countries are infringing on our fishing rights. There is no justice, no reason. Our country's fishermen are in great danger. Our country's fishermen are losing their livelihoods. Livelihoods are being cut off and we are becoming poor. There is not a single swallow flying down to the ground. The broken nets left by our grandfathers have all become useless things. Before long, all of our broken boats that can't move will be like sinking to the bottom, to the very bottom.

Qian Jingzhang, Qian Zuixian, Mao Jia Book

Zhongxi (1040) 10:00 AM to 10:45 AM

Opening "Garland of Flowers and Moon"

The spring river and flower moon are most prosperous. The moon reflects the flowers, and the flowers and moon accompany each other. Flowers love the bright moon, and the moon moves the shadows of the flowers. Flowers bloom awaiting the moon, and the zither ceases its sound. In the moon, drums urge on the flowers in a chaotic beat. Fallen flowers cover the ground like ten thousand golden characters. A crescent moon is like a jade hairpin. The flowery world is ever in spring. The monthly tide is never wrong. The bright moon is like a round jade axe. The plum blossoms play "Three Variations" on a bronze pipa. Jiang Lang's dreams revolve around a flower-producing brush. Zhang Ziyou wanders as an immortal on a moon raft. Face like a peach blossom, eyebrows like the moon. The moon in the water, the flower in the mirror. It is good to rely on the Old Man of the Moon to convey marriage contracts. Ask the flower servant to pick up the phoenix hairpin. Worshiping the moon and burning incense, feelings are sincere. Burying flowers and burying jade, regret is boundless. Reed flowers, autumn moon, the guest of Xunyang. A solitary moon and plum blossoms, the recluse's home. The moon palace sweeps away the excitement like a phoenix tail. The flower-covered steps are like phoenix-headed shoes in the moonlight. Trying to catch the moon in the water is futile talk. Appreciating flowers in the fog is inherently delightful. Leaning on the moon, yearning for someone, saddened by the moon pavilion. Wearing flowers in one's hair upon passing the imperial examination, strolling down the street. Chang'e lives in the lunar palace with osmanthus. The jade maiden wipes the water caltrop flower mirror. Wanting to roll up the bead curtain to cage the night moon. Deleting evil deeds to irrigate famous flowers. Fallen flowers, weeping birds, spring sorrow water. Slanting moon, dying lamp, night dreams.

"Famous Storytellers"

Sitting idly under the willows, hearing orioles sing. The spring flows murmuring, increasing the joy. Returning, composing tunes of industry and commerce. Writing about seventy famous storytellers. The oldest is Zhang Futian. The youngest is Yang Zhenxiong. The age difference between the two is fifty years. The Wei family is known as the three heroes. Wei Yuqing, the champion of the Pearl Pagoda. Has a younger brother, Junqing, and a son, Hanying. Shen Jian'an often partners with Xue Xiaoqing. Often calls for cigars, Chen Xuefang. Zhou Hanquan also sings "Jade Dragonfly." Yingying worships the moon, Huang Yian. Encountering Chen Shilin at Mi Xiang Village. Zhu Yaoting and Yaosheng, brothers, study the art of turning base metals into gold. Has a son who is an official, Zhu Jiesheng. Why burn the Hundred Flower Terrace? Wu Jianqiu is a rising young man. Zhao Jiaqiu married a Shanghai woman. Grandma, still goes to the dance hall at three o'clock. Xu Yunzhi goes to the garden, Grandfather Chen listens clearly to the servants' report. Yao Yinmei sings "A Stick of Snow," Zhu Yaoxiang wants a proper marriage. Xu Liulu, Hou Wanxia, Jiu Liu, Wu Xia, Qi Lianfang, Chen Lianqing, plus Zhao Hesheng. Du Wenkui is just like Qian Duzhao. Xu Xiaoyu, Chen Wenqing, are also junior members of the Wei family. Zhang Shaochan is skilled at playing the pipa. There is no second person in Shanghai. Zhou Zhenyu's Righteous Demon Legend

Yuan (1120) 12:45 AM to 1:30 AM

Opening "Nearsighted Eyes" (Mimi Collection Creative Issue)

Laughable are the gentleman's two eyes. He cannot see distant objects clearly. Mistaking the tree shadow by the wall for dry firewood to gather. Seeing a snake on the ground, he thinks it's a rotten straw rope. He broke the key when locking the bookcase. He burned his lips trying to blow out the lamp. Seeing a dragonfly hiding on the flower wall. He mistakes it for a good iron nail for a blunt net. Asking for directions, he comes across a clothing store. Seeing a wax statue in a Western suit, he smiles broadly. He calls him brother and bows deeply. Asks him which town or village he is heading to. Unexpectedly, the manufactured person does not understand. Stares blankly without a sound. Blaming him for looking down on people like a dog, he gets angry and furious. He knocks him down in the hall. The owner of the store gets inexplicably angry. Negotiating with him, blaming him. Even with an honest official, it cannot be clarified. Laughable, he runs into a black dog on the road. It bites him until he is covered in blood. He returns home and takes out the door bolt. Wanting to beat the enemy, he cannot. Coincidentally, there is a person mending a wok. Seeing it, he misunderstands immediately. He breaks the broken wok with a door bolt. Ending up losing money and feeling uneasy. Pitiable to have eyes that are as good as blind.

Sea Swallow Theater Company Seeking Male and Female Actors 264

The August 2nd performance has been postponed due to unforeseen circumstances. Replacing it with Gorky's "Burevestnik"

The Sea Swallow Theater Company had originally scheduled to perform "The Worker's Home," "A Way Out," "Night of Chaton," and "Colonial Storm," self-compiled by the company's members, four one-act plays on August 2nd. The plays have been rehearsed thoroughly. However, in the present situation where theatrical performances do not have freedom, their enthusiastic preparations for the August 2nd performance have had to be postponed due to certain reasons.

Now they have decided to abandon these four short plays and replace them with Gorky's "Burevestnik." In order to achieve some good results in the performance, they are publicly seeking several male and female actors for the play. Those who are between the ages of eighteen and thirty, have a considerable level of education, are physically fit, and can speak fluent Mandarin, can send their name, age, place of origin, experience, and attach a recent half-body and full-body photo to the company at No. 7 Huatongfang, Beixizang Road Bridge, this city. Those who are suitable will be contacted for an interview. Those who are not suitable will have their original letters returned. As for the performance aspect, a performance committee has been formed to take full responsibility for carrying it out.

Zhou Xuan, From Singing Stage to Silver Screen 265

— Photo by Xi Yuqun

Oriental Literature Published Today 266

Since its publication, Oriental Literature, edited by Hou Feng, has become very popular. It is heard that the fourth issue has been published today. The contents include ten articles by Guo Moruo and others commemorating Gorky, and Guo Moruo's "Opinions on National Defense Literature," Zheng Boqi's "Bloch's Literary View of the Nineteenth Century," and other papers, five creative works by Lie Gongshe and others, and essays by Yang Sao and others, and poems by Ms. An E, totaling over one hundred thousand words, which are distributed by the United Publishing House.

Introducing Child Star Shen Peihua 267

Shen Tianyin, manager of Yihua, has a daughter named Peihua, who is petite, exquisite, innocent, and adorable. Although she is three years old this year, she is actually not yet twenty-four months old. She has a naturally clever face, coupled with intelligent qualities, so although she is so young, her understanding of everything is astonishing. She is indeed a genius little treasure. She is currently making a guest appearance in Yue Feng's "Bao Baotu" (Treasure Map), playing the childhood role of Zhou Xuan. It is said that she has a lot of scenes and is very important. However, since filming began, she has never had a retake. She is calm and unafraid, handles everything with ease, and her excellent performance is even more amazing.
